1932.11.10

Today's Headlines

Domestic: Liu Xiang's Army Attacks Neijiang and Luzhou; Central Political Council Passes Proposal to Nationalize China Merchants Steam Navigation Company; Japanese Planes Bomb Nehe County Town

International: Roosevelt Elected President of the United States; Japan Expands Military Preparations; Japan-Russia Negotiations Reach a Deadlock

Shanghai Public Safety Bureau Held Winter Defense Conference Yesterday; Thirty-Three Major Criminals Plotting Against Political Figures Transferred to Public Safety Bureau; Order Banning Beixin Bookstore Books Issued to Shanghai

Commentary

Another Mystery: The US Presidential Election Unveiled

The heated competition of the US election over the past three months has officially come to an end today. After March next year, the master of the White House will not be the fifty-nine-year-old Hoover but the fifty-year-old Roosevelt.

The Republican Party has been steadily in power for twelve years since Harding took office in 1921 until now. Although the person in charge has changed three times during this period, the traditional policies have not changed slightly. Moreover, taking advantage of the shadow of the World War, they believe that the prosperity of the United States of America will continue for ten thousand years and forever maintain its absolute victory. However, the stock market crash in the autumn of 1929 suddenly occurred, and the so-called Hoover market plummeted and could not be recovered. Although various stimulating methods have been used from last year to the present to incite the market to turn for the better, they have been ineffective. Especially after July this year, they have tried their best to encourage stock prices to rise. Although it has risen by several points, it has never reached the prosperous state of 1929. Therefore, it is increasingly known that the Republican Party's inability to grasp the hearts of the people is already obvious.

Now that Democratic presidential candidate Roosevelt has been elected, the platform he has put forward will be implemented in the future. In addition to the repeal of Prohibition, which can be implemented in a short period of time, other domestic economic policies will inevitably feel thorny.

First, the United States has been deeply affected by the economic panic. Although there are no accurate official statistics on the number of unemployed people, according to various professional estimates, it should be at least over 11 million. This is actually the biggest difficulty facing the United States and a common crisis shared by capitalist countries. Mr. Roosevelt promised to provide jobs for the unemployed when he was campaigning. However, it is difficult for American industry in general to suddenly prosper because of Mr. Roosevelt's election. Then, after he takes office as president, how can he have jobs to give to people who have no work to do? Moreover, the turning point of the world economy has not yet seen a real turnaround. Mr. Roosevelt himself may not be able to turn the tide single-handedly.

Second, the long-standing disputes between Europe and the United States are attached to the war debt related to the German reparations issue. The principal and interest of the debts owed by European countries to the United States total about 22 billion US dollars. The Republican Party originally adopted a procrastinating attitude toward this issue, perhaps fearing that it would be too obvious. Whether it is cancellation or collection, it will cause huge storms at home and abroad. The Democratic Party sings against the "cancellation of war debts," even if it wins the sympathy of domestic capitalists, or can stimulate the excitement of the public debt stock market, but the European countries' economic crisis and the "cash preference" and other complex intertwined relationships in the rescue of the world economic panic, even if the United States decides not to recognize the cancellation of war debts, what if the debtor countries are unable to repay?

Third, on the issue of tariffs, the Democratic Party platform states: 'The purpose is to have revenue tariffs for competition that are not subject to the interference of the executive branch, to establish a new fact-finding committee, to conclude reciprocal tariff agreements with various countries, and to promote world economic conferences to increase trade and make exchange transactions easier.' Mr. Roosevelt also attacked the Republican Party's protectionist tariff policy as much as possible during his campaign. However, both historically and in reality, the Democratic Party is not a free trade advocate but a considerable protectionist. The difference between the Democratic and Republican parties is only in degree. Moreover, the eastern, western, central, southern, and northern parts of the United States have different industrial and economic interests and viewpoints, making it difficult to reach a consensus. Therefore, although the Democratic Party advocates reciprocal agreements, how effective is its implementation? There is no doubt. Moreover, after the British Imperial Economic Conference, the economic alliance within the British Empire seems to be gradually forming. At this time, would it be easy to conclude a reciprocal tariff agreement with other countries that sacrifices their own country? Mr. Roosevelt cannot but be concerned about this.

Fourth, foreign policy issues did not occupy a special position in this US competitive election, meaning that there is no major difference between the two parties' foreign policies. Their main focus is on the Far East issue. Regardless of the Republican or Democratic parties, their policies toward China and their attitudes toward the Pacific hegemony are very similar. Moreover, they all advocate maintaining the Washington Nine-Power Treaty and the Kellogg-Briand Pact. They all hold the same attitude toward the preservation of China's territorial integrity, the open door, and equal opportunity. They also adhere to the "non-recognition doctrine" regarding Japan's invasion of Manchuria. The Democratic Party is no different in this regard.

We recall that when Japan forced China to recognize the Twenty-One Demands in 1915, the then-President of the United States was Wilson, who was a Democrat. His Secretary of State, Mr. Bryan, sent a letter to Japan on May 13 stating, "The treaty rights of the United States and American people in China, the territorial and political integrity of China, and the general open door, if any agreement detrimental to international policy is concluded between China and Japan, the United States cannot recognize it." This "non-recognition doctrine" has never been changed from Wilson to Hoover. Mr. Roosevelt, who comes from the Democratic Party, although there are some differences between his domestic policies and his relationship with European war debts and the Republican Party, the tradition of his Far East policy is difficult and impossible to change both in terms of momentum and reason. However, it may replace Mr. Stimson's verbal protests with actual preparations. Although Mr. Roosevelt has been engaged in the peace movement in recent years and is not as soaring as when he was Undersecretary of the Navy, he is also a practical politician. Although the Democratic Party advocates the independence of the Philippines, it has not allowed it to abandon its military privileges in the Philippines. It can still establish a strong naval fleet in the western Pacific. Therefore, in addition to giving the American people a drink to their heart's content, the master of the White House after March next year still needs to work hard. We sincerely wish Mr. Roosevelt well on his election as the new president of the United States.

Important News

Japanese Planes Bomb Nehe County Town

Tang Juyuwu Supervises the Battle in Mudanjiang

Japanese Troops Stationed in Chaoyang Temple Withdraw to Shenyang

(Beiping) Ma Zhanshan telegraphed from Beiping on the 4th, saying that three enemy planes suddenly came to Nehe County Town at noon on the 1st and circled for several weeks. The next day, a large number of planes came again and dropped heavy bombs on civilian houses, totaling more than 20, and released poison gas bombs with the intention of slaughtering everything. It is found that this kind of cruel trick by the Japanese army violates international law and is truly inhumane. Please announce it to China and foreign countries as soon as possible so that the truth can be known.

Tang Juyuwu Supervises the Battle in Mudanjiang

(Beiping) After Tang Juyuwu's troops temporarily retreated to the Mudanjiang area, the Japanese side has been pressing forward step by step recently. The morale is extremely high. The headquarters and affiliated agencies are temporarily set up in Mudanjiang to engage in the connection of friendly forces and plan for further development. There are still fierce battles between the two sides in Liaoning, Hailong, Jinchuan, and Fusong counties. Tang Juyuwu personally supervises the battle in Mudanjiang.

(Beiping) Tang Juyuwu sent a telegram requesting an end to the civil war so that the national crisis could be eliminated and the lost territory could be recovered as soon as possible. (Special telegram on the 9th)

Three Thousand Volunteer Soldiers Once Occupied Shuangcheng

(Harbin) According to Japanese sources, the train protected by Japanese soldiers will only run to Hailin from today onwards and will not go to Shitoutouzi. Hailin is about 200 miles west of Harbin. According to Russian newspapers here, 3,000 volunteer soldiers once occupied Shuangcheng on November 6. When the "Manchukuo" garrison retreated,

they encountered Japanese troops traveling from Changchun to Harbin and jointly attacked Shuangcheng, driving away the volunteer soldiers. It is reported that many civilians were killed. (Reuters telegram on the 8th)

Japanese Troops Stationed in Manchuria Disarmed

(Tokyo) According to a report from the Japanese consul in Matsievskaya, Russia, 38 Japanese people, including five women, at the Japanese plenipotentiary's office in Changchun are still detained in Manzhouli. In addition, there are 125 Manchurian officials. The commander of the railway protection army summoned Captain Uno, the commander of the Japanese troops, to his headquarters on September 27 and demanded that Uno disarm his troops. Uno believed that the lives of Japanese residents were in danger, so he agreed on the condition of guaranteeing the safety of the lives and property of Japanese residents. Therefore, Uno and the Japanese consul Yamazaki were allowed to return to the consulate. (Reuters telegram on the 9th)

Pu Bingshan's Army Closes in on Tai'an

(Beiping) Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang People's Support Association received a telegram from the commissioner of Qiqihar on the 6th, saying that the main force of Pu Bingshan's troops, 3,000 men, engaged in a fierce battle with the Japanese Kuroda and Unmura divisions five miles east of Taian Town for five hours. The Japanese were defeated and retreated. Pu's army captured five field guns, five mortars, six machine guns, and nine boxes of ammunition. The advance team has pressed under the city of Tai'an, etc. I especially heard about it. (Special telegram on the 9th)

Wang Delin's Troops Advance Towards Qihe

(Beiping) Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang People's Support Association received a telegram from the special commissioner of Jilin, saying that on the 26th of last month, the Japanese side dispatched 500 railway protection troops carrying lumber workers to rush to repair the Jihui railway line. Wu Yicheng, led by Wang Delin, led more than 1,000 volunteer soldiers to ambush and intercept at a certain place (code name unknown) and hit the enemy's vehicle with hand grenades. The gasoline exploded at that time, and the Japanese troops fled and were surrounded by ambush troops. After a fierce battle, all the enemy troops were wiped out. In this battle, the enemy captured nine machine guns, more than 950 rifles, two mountain guns, four chase guns, and eleven boxes of bullets. On the 4th of this month, Wang's troops had occupied Hengdaohezi. The Japanese and rebel armies suffered 270 casualties. Wang's troops suffered 70 casualties. They are now advancing towards Qihe, etc. I especially heard about it. (Telegram on the 9th)

Volunteer Soldiers Hold Near Jinzhou

(Shanhaiguan) The volunteer army near Liangpeng Mountain in northern Jinzhou once attacked Jinzhou and is now holding on to wait for an opportunity. On the 5th, Japanese planes bombed the nearby miscellaneous woodland, Zicun, and Waiboshuzhuang, all of which were burned down. The morale of the volunteer army is still extremely high and they are determined to resist the enemy to the death. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Shanhaiguan) Except for the railway and the three districts near the county seat, the remaining five districts in the eight districts under the jurisdiction of Suizhong County are currently occupied by the volunteer army.

Japanese Barracks in Suizhong Completed

(Beiping) The Japanese barracks built in Suizhong were completed. The commander of the Japanese Kwantung Army sent Captain Hashikawa to inspect and hold a military parade. Suizhong has a large artillery platform and a watchtower, and the military deployment is extremely strict. (Special telegram on the 9th)

Volunteer Soldiers Attack Lianshan for Days

(Beiping) The volunteer army attacking Lianshan has been attacking near Lianshan for days. The Japanese army has an armored train at Lianshan Station, which uses giant cannons to shoot eastward from time to time. The nearby rural areas have been completely destroyed, and the victims are fleeing everywhere. (Special telegram on the 9th)

Japanese Troops in Chaoyang Temple Transferred to Jinzhou

(Beiping) 80 of the Japanese troops stationed in Chaoyang Temple were transferred to Jinzhou on the 8th, and more than 100 people were transferred back to Shenyang for rest. Another squadron of Matsumoto, about 100 people, was transferred from Goubangzi to take over. (Special telegram on the 9th)

An Da's Rebel Army Defects Entirely

(Beiping) Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang People's Support Association received a telegram from the commissioner of Harbin, saying that a certain unit (code name unknown) of the Manchurian army at An Da Station, 6,500 men, defected entirely on the 6th of this month due to the pain of the Japanese army's brutal oppression. They are now united with the Soviet army to attack the Japanese army. The Japanese army is panicked and showing signs of retreat. All commerce in northern Manchuria has been suspended. The Japanese army only controls the eastern section of the Chinese Eastern Railway to the Nu'er River and the western section to Fularji. The Japanese side has temporarily suspended the attack on the Nenjiang Bridge because the Chinese army's positions in the Hinggan Mountains are strong and many Manchurian troops have defected. Li Du and Ding Chao are now building a new government in northern Jilin and eastern Heilongjiang and issuing their own paper money, etc. (Special telegram on the 9th)

Rebel Troops Stationed in Tao'an Prepare to Withdraw

(Beiping) Liu Zhendong of the Liaoning National Salvation Army telegraphed from the 7th, saying that the Japanese side feared that our army would attack Taonan and cut off its Siping-Taonan railway traffic, so it withdrew the troops stationed in Jilin and Heilongjiang to consolidate Changchun. The Zhang Haipeng troops of the rebel army stationed in Tao'an are grabbing cars everywhere to prepare to withdraw. If our army has winter clothes, it can approach Taonan quickly. Please transport leather clothes quickly. (Special telegram on the 9th)

Liu Xiang's Army Attacks Luzhou and Neijiang

Mu Yingzhou's Troops Attack Luzhou City Fiercely

The Two Armies in Neijiang Are at a Stalemate

Deng Tian Still Advocates Convening a Suining Conference

(Hankou) Mu Yingzhou attacked Luzhou, shooting from the south bank across the river. The Liao and He troops launched a fierce attack on the city on the 7th under the cover of two warships. The battle was fierce on the 8th. One Chongqing warship was destroyed by artillery fire. The Chongqing army in Neijiang retreated as soon as they came into contact. They are now at a stalemate. Liu Xiang plans to take Luzhou first, take Fushun, and then attack Zizhong. Now there is a change in the plan, saying that the battle near Gaoshikan in Fushun is also fierce and the outcome is undecided. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Nanjing) Chongqing telegram: 1. The war in eastern Sichuan is about to enter an intense period. The Allied forces are attacking Liu Wenhui's defense area in three routes. One is to attack Luzhou from Yongchuan, one is to attack Neijiang from Longchang, which is the main force of the Chongqing army, and one is to attack Zizhou from Anshan, which is under the command of the Daotian, Yang, Li, and Luo units. Liu Wenhui is determined to defend Zizhong, Fushun, Luzhou, and other places, which are the lifeline of his army. The outcome of the two sides will be determined in this battle. 2. In the battle of Zizhong, the vanguard of the Allied forces has occupied the first line of skirmishers of the provincial army. The Chongqing army is determined to attack Luzhou with all its strength and then completely block the traffic to Chengdu. 3. The Chongqing army's He Liuxiu brigade fiercely attacked Luzhou City on the 7th and has now stopped on the 8th. Liu Wenhui has transferred all the rear troops to Zizhong and Luzhou and ordered the garrison commander Tian Brigade Commander to defend to the death and not retreat. Liu Wenhui will arrive in Luzhou today to supervise the battle. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Hankou) Zhang Qun talked on the 9th that he had met Jiang on the evening of the 8th, but did not talk about Sichuan. Now that the war has been launched for a long time, it is difficult to solve it immediately. However, the plan to find a way to prevent it from expanding and prolonging it until the Sichuan situation is permanently stabilized should first seek the crux of the Sichuan chaos, such as military, political, and financial disunity, which have been the source of chaos for many years. A thorough reorganization should be carried out. The order issued by the National Government in the 17th year of the Republic of China can still be applied. I am studying its implementation. I will discuss it with Jiang in detail to facilitate its smooth progress. If I need to go to Sichuan, I will not hesitate to do so, but now is not the time. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Nanjing) Tian Songyao's representatives Wang Shuren and Xie Zimin said that the union of Deng, Tian, and Liu is purely propaganda from a certain party. This kind of rumor was true two years ago. The Sichuan situation has now evolved into a survival competition between the various armies and Liu Wenhui. This is absolutely not the case. Tian has always followed the central government's will in governing the army in Sichuan. At this time, when the entire Sichuan army and people are jointly seeking to improve the Sichuan situation, they should adhere to their original intentions and work together to achieve a thorough solution in a short period of time to relieve the central government's concerns in the west. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Hankou) Liu Xiang's subordinate Pan Wenhua's division attacked Neijiang and has arrived at Xiaoshi, saying that Mu Yingzhou and others attacked Lanzhou and have arrived at Dongjiezi. Both are separated from Liu Wenhui's troops by a small river. The battle has been fierce since the 8th. Chongqing planes often arrive in the provincial army's defense area and drop bombs, causing considerable casualties among the people. Liu Xiang will not accept any advice from any party until Luzhou and Neijiang are taken. Liu Wenhui has also ordered all units to defend to the death and seek an opportunity to counterattack to win the victory and issued air defense measures to be observed by the military and civilians. Deng Tian has always been consistent, on the one hand, supporting Liu Wenhui's plan to govern Sichuan, and on the other hand, still advocating the convening of the Suining Conference. Deng's troops have been transferred to Zizhong, and it is rumored that they will help Chengdu resist Chongqing. (Special telegram on the 9th)

Yexian and Laiyang Will Be Relieved Tomorrow

Zhang Fang Departs from Jinan to Hankou to Report to Jiang

Liu Zhennian's Troops Will Be Transferred to Suixian and Zaoyang for Garrison

(Jinan) Han Fuju telegraphed to all parties reporting the withdrawal from Yantai, briefly stating that according to Cao Fulin, the division commander, Qi Wei did not telegraph, saying that the navy had arrived in Yantai late yesterday. Huang Zhizhong's regiment had completed the handover of the defense area and everything else in Yantai this morning and set off along the Yantai-Weifang line to return to Yexian at 10:00 am this morning. The local area was very peaceful before leaving Yantai, etc. I especially telegraphed to report. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Jinan) Han talked about Huang Zhizhong's regiment, which can arrive in Huangxian from Yantai today, can arrive in Yexian on the 10th, and Yexian and Laiyang can be relieved at the same time on the 11th. The large-scale layoffs and salary reductions in this province are due to financial difficulties, but how to implement them is still under discussion. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Jinan) Zhang Fang, Liu Yaoyang, and Zhang Yue returned to Jinan from Qingdao today. All the important people arrived at the station to welcome Zhang Fang. Zhang will return to Hankou to report to Jiang on the process of resolving the Shandong issue. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Jinan) Shahe telegram: Zhang Shoujing, the section chief of the headquarters' staff office, came to Shahe yesterday with Han's order, detailing the steps for withdrawing troops and the deployment after the withdrawal. The brigade commanders Li Hanzhang, Li Yizhi, Ma Guanyi, Chen Dexin, and Rong Guangxing are discussing the troop withdrawal plan with the division commander Cao Fulin in Shahe. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Jinan) Song Shishan, the supervisor sent by Zhang Xueliang, passed through Shahe to Yantai at noon on the 9th. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Jinan) Zhang Fang and Liu Yaoyang are scheduled to return to Henan tonight. Zhang will go to Hankou to report to Jiang. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Jinan) Shahe telegram: The Huang regiment, which withdrew from Yantai, has now passed Huangxian Longkou. The cavalry brigade Li Xuande's troops may arrive in Shahe on the 10th or 11th. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Jinan) Lu Bangjian telegraphed to Xiong Bin, saying that he arrived in Yecheng at 3:00 pm on the 7th and had a very satisfactory conversation with Division Commander Liu. All the procedures regarding the transfer of defense are in accordance with the orders of the central government. Other issues have also been properly resolved. My mission in Jinan has been completed. I hope you will come soon. Division Commander Liu also extends a warm welcome. Reply by telegram, please transfer from Nanjing. Xiong talked about Yu, and I have telegraphed Liu to inform him that the three-way army in Yexian and Laiyang can withdraw on the 12th. The military department ordered him to transfer the defense. I think the order has been received. Please prepare to set off. I am sure to go to Yexian on the 11th. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Hankou) Liu Zhennian telegraphed from Hankou on the 8th: 1. Xiong Bin's secretary, Lu Bangjian, arrived in Yexian on the 7th. Xiong will come soon. 2. In order to avoid the suffering of the people, this division asks to be transferred out of Shandong. I hope more ships will be dispatched for transportation. 3. The Han army in Yexian and Laiyang still shows no signs of withdrawing. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Beiping) He Yingqin telegraphed to Jiang Bocheng and Xiong Bin to first transfer Zhennian's troops to Huayuan Station on the Ping-Han Railway and then to Zaoyang and Suixian. Liu's troops still have 8,000 men. After Liu's troops are transferred, the defense of the counties in Jiaodong will be taken over by the provincial army. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Nanjing) Liu Zhennian's troops will begin to be transferred on the 15th. The route has been decided by the Military and Political Department. They will land in Haizhou and transfer to the Ping-Han train to Hankou. The Hubei, Henan, and Anhui Bandit Suppression Headquarters has drawn up the location of Liu's troops. After concentrating in Hankou, they will be transferred to Macheng and Suixian in eastern Hubei to carry out bandit suppression work. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Jinan) At 8:00 pm, Zhang Fang's special train left Jinan, first to Hanchuan and then to Hankou to report to Jiang. Han and Jiang Bocheng, Xiong Bin, and other important people went to the station to see him off. Liu Yaoyang will go to Beiping from Jinan. (Special telegram on the 9th)

Central Political Council Passes Proposal to Nationalize China Merchants Steam Navigation Company

Order the Ministry of Communications to Formulate an Organization and Reorganization Plan

The Reorganization List Has Been Determined: General Manager Liu Hongsheng

(Nanjing) The Central Political Council held its 331st meeting on the morning of the 9th. The members present were Chen Guofu, Ye Chucang, Ju Zheng, Chen Gongbo, Zeng Zhongming, Tang Youren, Shao Yuanchong, He Yaozu, Zhao Pilian, Chen Shuren, Zhu Jiahua, Zhou Qigang, Shi Ying, Dai Jialun, Miao Peicheng, and more than 20 others. Chen Guofu presided over the meeting and decided on the following important cases: 1. The draft revision of the organization regulations of the Reflection Institute will be submitted to the Political Report Group and the Legal System Group for review. 2. The Executive Yuan requested that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company be nationalized and all shares be recovered by the state at the recent average market price with cash, inheriting the original rights and legal debts of the company, reorganizing the board of directors and supervisors, and establishing a general manager to select reputable people from all walks of life to thoroughly plan and create a modern enterprise. The application should be approved and the Executive Yuan should order the Ministry of Communications to formulate the organization law and reorganization plan of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and submit it for approval. 3. Approved seven budget proposals. 4. The fishery issue will be submitted to the Ministry of Industry for detailed planning and submitted to this meeting for review. (Central News Agency telegram on the 9th)

(Nanjing) Ministry of Communications Information: The reorganization list of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is as follows: General Manager Liu Hongsheng, Standing Directors Ye Zhuotang, Liu Hongsheng, Shi Liangcai, Zhang Shouyong, Zhang Jiaao, Du Yong, Yang Ying, and seven others. Directors Hu Bijang, Li Ming, Wang Xiaolai, Qian Yongming, Yu Rizhang, Zhang Yin, Hu Junzhuang, Sheng Shengyi, and eight others. Supervisors Lu Xuepu, Chen Guangfu, Yu Hede, Hu Zutong, Qin Zuze, Rong Zongjing, Huang Jinrong, Jin Tingsun, Guo Shun, and nine others have been sent to the Government Civil Affairs Office by the Executive Yuan to be submitted to the President for appointment. (Special telegram on the 9th)

(Nanjing) The Central Political Council reported on the morning of the 9th that the Financial Group reviewed the following cases: 1. The special case of the Ministry of Industry requesting early disbursement of the 20th year's recurring budget for the Shanghai-Hankou Commodity Inspection Bureau and the Central Industrial Testing Institute. 2. The Ministry of Industry's Jiangsu and Zhejiang Fishery Administration Bureau and its affiliated patrol ships' 20th year's additional recurring budget. 3. The monthly budget of the Mongolian and Tibetan Xunbao for the 20th year. 4. The additional temporary budget of the Nanjing Technical Cooperation Committee for the 20th year. 5. The recurring budget of the Forensic Research Institute directly under the Ministry of Justice and Administration for the 21st year, which was forwarded by the government. It was decided that all opinions should be approved. 6. The Industrial Gazette compiled by the Ministry of Industry and the temporary budget of the Fujian and Guangdong Marine Fishery Administration Bureau for the 21st year. It was decided that 1. The budget for compiling the Industrial Gazette should be approved. 2. The recurring temporary budget of the Fujian and Guangdong Marine Fishery Administration Bureau should be reviewed after the Ministry of Industry sends personnel to investigate the local situation and decide whether the agency needs to be established immediately. (Special telegram on the 9th)

Control Yuan Decides to Impeach Case of Sale of Objects from the Forbidden City

(Nanjing) Yu Youren of the Control Yuan will return to Beijing from Shanghai next Saturday. Before the previous month, the hospital reviewed an average of more than 60 cases of all sizes every day and sent people to Shanghai at any time. The Control Yuan believes that the case of ancient objects from the Forbidden City must be impeached. It is found that before the sale of the right objects, the committee issued printed materials explaining the reasons, saying that the ancient objects sold were 1. Those that have nothing to do with culture, 2. Those that are about to rot, 3. Those that are incomplete. However, according to the facts, a large number of gold utensils were sold, and more than 70 gold shops in Beiping competed to buy them. They were temporarily sold by the catty. It is conceivable that the weight of the large gold utensils sold was large. The price sold is only 30% of the current gold market. Even if the manufacturing cost of the gold utensils in the past is not counted, the reduction of gold materials according to the current market price is extremely inappropriate. At present, the Control Yuan has ordered the two committees Gao Lu and Zhou Lisheng to go to Beiping on the first day of this month to investigate. Once the evidence is confirmed, Yi Peiji and others, the directors of the Ancient Objects Preservation Committee of the Forbidden City, will be impeached. (Special telegram on the 9th)

Song Dai Meets Jiang in Hankou

(Hankou) Dai Chuanxian and Song Ziwen met Jiang on the morning of the 9th. Dai then went to Zhongshan Park to talk to the city's Boy Scouts. Song Ziwen received Zhang Xueliang's representative Bao Wenwei and Liu Zhennian's representative Han Dong at the Bank of China at noon. Song crossed the river to visit Luojia Mountain and visited Xia Douyin. He returned to Hankou in the evening. It is said that he will fly to Beijing on the 10th and will return to Beijing after meeting Yu Xuezong. Zhang Yinxiang and Yue Sen visited Jiang on the 9th, and Chen Jicheng went to Shanghai. (Special telegram on the 9th)

Important Telegram 2

French Envoy's Activities in Beijing

The Vietnam Treaty Will Be Resubmitted for Revision

(Nanjing) French Envoy Wilden met with Tieci and Zeng Zhongwu at the French Embassy's Beijing Office on the morning of the 9th, and then at 11:00 AM, accompanied by Counselor Baude, visited Naval Minister Chen Shaokuan. In the afternoon, he visited Minister of Industry and Commerce Chen Gongbo for a long discussion. He planned to meet with Luo Wengan again on the 10th to discuss issues related to the Sino-French-Vietnamese border trade agreement and other Sino-French matters. According to the French envoy, most of the Sino-French-Vietnamese border trade agreement has already been signed, with only the list of taxable goods and other procedures remaining. He hoped that after consultations with Chinese diplomatic authorities, they could be agreed upon. Regarding the League of Nations' discussion of the Sino-Japanese incident, he expressed that while he had considerable opinions, he was unable to express them publicly before a detailed meeting with Chinese diplomatic authorities. Envoy Wilden only brought Secretary Gigout with him on this trip and will not stay in Beijing for long before heading to Shanghai. (9th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Sino-French-Vietnamese trade agreement, after being revised and signed on May 16, 1930, has not yet been promulgated by the French government due to issues such as the Yunnan surtax and Longzhou. As a result, Chinese expatriates in Vietnam are in a position of not having treaty protections, and the goods they import are subject to heavy taxes by the French, causing severe hardship and decline for Chinese businesses. Representatives Huang An and Xu Yixian of the South Vietnamese Chamber of Commerce returned to China to petition, and they met with a certain gentleman in the Foreign Ministry who said that French Envoy Wilden had come to Beijing from Beiping a few days ago and had already held one round of talks with Foreign Minister Luo. Currently, the agreement will be resubmitted for revision, and the Foreign Ministry is currently studying it. The main points of the revision will be the issue of the list of imported goods and the basis for the exchange of notes between Zhu Zhaoxin of Guangdong and Lagarde. Regarding the tariff aspects, the Foreign Ministry has already consulted the Ministry of Finance on the 9th, requesting them to send personnel to jointly study the matter so that the agreement can be concluded as soon as possible. (9th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) It is rumored that the Foreign Ministry will consult with the French envoy on implementing the new Vietnam treaty. When asked by reporters, Zhang Weihan, the Secretary-General of the Legislative Yuan who participated in the agreement, stated that, in his observation, the French side's attitude towards China has been very good recently, and Envoy Wilden has also made great efforts to promote Sino-French friendship. He believes that his arrival in Beijing will allow him to understand China's hopes and urge the French government to implement the treaty as soon as possible. (9th Dispatch)

Zhu Jia骅 Concurrently Manages Educational Affairs

(Nanjing) Minister of Education Weng Wenhao declined to take office, and Zhu Jia骅 will temporarily manage the ministry's affairs until a formal candidate is decided after the Third Plenary Session. (9th Dispatch)

Ministry of Interior Strictly Enforces Measures to Prohibit the Keeping of Slaves and Maids

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Interior has stipulated measures to prohibit the keeping of slaves and maids. The keeping of slaves and maids not in an employment relationship, regardless of whether through purchase, gift, or charitable means, is prohibited. The steps to be taken are: 1. Persuasion, 2. Emancipation, 3. Relief, and 4. Punishment. The directly administered municipal governments and the municipalities and counties under the jurisdiction of each province are to be instructed by the provincial and municipal governments to conduct thorough investigations through the police authorities and implement the measures in accordance with the steps. As for relief methods: 1. Unmarried slaves and maids who have a home to return to should be sent home. If they have no home to return to or their family members are unable to support them, they should be sent to the local relief home. If there is no relief home, they should be sent to a charitable organization. 2. Adult slaves and maids, regardless of gender, should be allowed to freely choose a spouse and seek other employment opportunities. Punishment methods should be handled by the judicial authorities in accordance with Article 313 of the Criminal Law, which deals with the crime of enslaving people. The slaves and maids kept should be forcibly emancipated and a fine of up to 300 yuan should be imposed. (9th Dispatch)

Zheng Tianxi Discusses the Shanghai Special Court Agreement

(Nanjing) Deputy Foreign Minister Zheng Tianxi stated that the report that the British Chargé d'Affaires in China was discussing the revision of the Shanghai Special District Court Agreement with the government was incorrect, as the ministry had not discussed the matter with him. As to whether the matter had been discussed with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, he was not aware of it. Currently, the case is being handled by the Revision Agreement Committee jointly established by this ministry and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Once it reaches a certain stage, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will notify the relevant countries to propose revisions. The government will naturally negotiate cautiously based on the principle of recovering legal rights. It is expected that revisions will begin when the three-year term expires next March. (9th Dispatch)

Most of the Censorate's Impeachment Cases Have Been Delayed

(Nanjing) Although the main culprit in the Shuangqing Smuggling Case has escaped, the Censorate has not abandoned the case. As Chairman Chiang is handling the case in Hankou, it is expected to be investigated and handled through political means. The impeachment case against Chairman Xiong Shihui of Jiangxi Province has already been filed, and the current focus is on the Yangzhou land tax incident, which is being thoroughly investigated and will also be subject to impeachment. Those holding specially appointed positions who are impeached are dealt with by the Central Government Officials' Disciplinary Committee. However, the public officials' disciplinary committees of the various courts have been established for half a year, and the Censorate has sent a total of more than 140 impeachment cases, but only four cases have been executed by the committee. Among the four cases, two were sent back to the original agencies for execution, so only two cases have actually been executed. This is because the members of the committee are all legal professionals and each case must be handled in accordance with legal procedures, which causes delays and wastes time. In fact, the penalties for impeachment cases are only three types: 1. salary deduction, 2. dismissal, and 3. removal from office, and there is no criminal penalty. As for the regulations for the Central Government Officials' Disciplinary Committee, it has not yet been formally established. It is planned to have 30 members directly under the National Government, and the members will be appointed by the Chairman of the National Government, consisting of Central Supervisory Committee members and Central Political Council members. Currently, there are more than 80 impeachment cases of specially appointed officials that have been approved by the Censorate and are awaiting execution. They will all be handed over to the committee for execution once it is established. (9th Dispatch)

Capital Residents Pay Attention to the US Elections

(Nanjing) After hearing the news of the US elections, Chinese officials said that regardless of which party is elected, the American people will demonstrate justice and fairness in their foreign policy, and that Roosevelt is deeply familiar with East Asian affairs and will be able to formulate a foreign policy regarding the situation in the Far East based on the Kellogg-Briand Pact and the Nine-Power Treaty to maintain world peace. (9th Reuters Dispatch)

(Nanjing) People here are paying close attention to the results of the US elections today. The Chinese people have never paid so much attention to foreign elections as they have this time. This is because the League of Nations is about to convene, and the US representative on the Lytton Commission will also participate in the discussions. The relationship between the US and the future development of the Sino-Japanese issue is very important. General opinion is that US foreign policy, especially Far Eastern policy, will not change due to a change in government. (9th Reuters Dispatch)

Fujian Provincial Government Convenes a Financial Conference

Issues 200,000 Yuan in Promissory Notes from the Finance Department

(Fuzhou) Today, the provincial government convened a joint meeting of party, government, military, business, and banking representatives to discuss the province's financial problems. Fang Shengxun reported on the hardships of maintaining the situation, and finally it was decided that the Finance Department would issue 200,000 yuan in promissory notes. Officials and merchants would be responsible for discounting them to alleviate various urgent needs. (9th Dispatch)

(Hankou) The Highway Conference held its fifth meeting on the 9th, and all proposals have been fully discussed. It will be completed in the future, and it will be of great benefit to military, political, and economic affairs. The conference will close at 10:00 AM tomorrow, and Chiang Kai-shek has decided to participate in the instruction. (9th Dispatch)

Preliminary Hearing Held for Opium Smuggling Case

(Nanjing) Wang Dawei, the presiding judge of the Criminal Court of the Jiangning District Court, held a preliminary hearing at 2 PM on the 9th for the case of Fan Guorui, a staff member of the National Government's Military Advisory Office, and others, who were involved in smuggling opium. The lawyers hired by Fan, Liu Zhe and Liu Bochang, appeared in court to defend him. First, Fan Guorui, Ren Zhongkun (orderly of the Chief Military Advisor), and Wang Jisan (manager of the Luoyang Sino-Western Hotel) were brought to court for individual questioning. The testimonies of the three were extremely cunning, each trying to shirk responsibility. Then, the three were brought face to face in court. Each side insisted on their own account of events, and the arguments were heated. The two lawyers also presented counter-evidence to defend Fan: 1) The authenticity of the writing on the calling card has not been confirmed; a re-evaluation is requested. 2) In the Luoyang Sino-Western Hotel, Ren Zhongkun said Fan was wearing a gray cloth military uniform, while Wang Jisan said he was wearing a white gown. The two testimonies are obviously contradictory, suggesting Ren Zhongkun intentionally framed Fan. 3) Wang Jisan did not confirm that Fan Guorui was an accomplice, so this cannot be considered evidence of a crime. 4) After the opium was transported to Beijing, Fan immediately reported to Section Chief Xiao Qin. If Fan was indeed an accomplice, he would have kept it a secret. Why would he dare to report it? 5) Section Chief Xiao should be summoned to testify in court. 6) In addition, Fan's colleague, Xiao Lan, was also present and should be summoned to testify. After the lawyers' arguments, the presiding judge declared that the case still required investigation and ordered the three defendants to be detained and the hearing postponed to a later date. (9th Dispatch)

Beijing Municipal Government Forms Property Tax Review Committee

(Nanjing) In order to resolve property tax disputes, the municipal government has formed a temporary Property Tax Review Committee. Secretary-General Lai Lian was appointed as the chairman, and the heads of various bureaus were appointed as members. The first meeting was held on the 9th, establishing the following work priorities: 1. Determine the principles for resolving property tax disputes. 2. Review past dispute cases. According to those who participated in the discussion, in the entire city of over 100,000 households, since the residential property tax exemption was set at four yuan or less, and above four yuan at 5%, and business property tax exemption was set at two yuan or less, and above two yuan at 10% in the 18th year of the Republic [1929], there has been no change to date. This time, it was discovered that the number of households evading taxes exceeded 40%, so in order to reorganize finances and equalize the burden on the people, it was necessary to reorganize the system. (9th Dispatch)

Investigation and Prohibition of Insulting-China Movie Screenings

(Nanjing) The Ministries of Interior and Education have approved a dispatch from the embassy in Belgium stating that the Paramount Film Company of the United States is still showing the film "Shanghai Express," which insults the Chinese nation, in various places in Europe. Overseas Chinese are indignant and have requested negotiations to ban it. The Film Censorship Committee of the Ministries of Interior and Education severely reprimanded Shanghai Paramount again on the 7th, setting a deadline for destroying the film; otherwise, the company's film inspections will be suspended. On the 9th, the Chinese and Western manager of Paramount came to Nanjing to lobby, but to no avail. (9th Dispatch)

Joint Government-Business Alcohol Factory

(Nanjing) Liu Haiping, Director of the Industry Department of the Ministry of Industry, told reporters that the alcohol factory planned by the Ministry is a joint government-business venture with a capital of 250,000 yuan, with government funds accounting for more than 100,000 yuan and commercial shares. Several discussions have been held with Shanghai merchants, and preparations are underway. Currently, the source of raw materials is being surveyed to determine the factory site. (9th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Recommendation to Expedite Banking Law

(Nanjing) Chen Changheng spoke about the Legislative Yuan's recommendation to the Central Political Council to expedite the formulation of the Bank Exchange Certificate Issuance Law and the Central Bank Law. The Central Political Council decided to hand it over to the Executive Yuan for drafting. The reason is that the issuance of banknotes by banks should be subject to government supervision to avoid excessive issuance and affecting the national economy. Therefore, laws must be formulated. In addition to the Central Bank, there are approximately two types of banks in our country: 1) joint government-business ventures; 2) provincial banks. The latter is prone to abuses due to a lack of restrictions. For example, Feng banknotes and Shanxi banknotes have become impossible to cash. In view of the current situation, the total amount of banknotes from each bank is approximately 500 million, while the capital of the Central Bank is only 20 million. It is impossible to concentrate all the debts of each bank to the nation. Furthermore, although the Central Bank has been established for several years, it is only based on the previous single regulations promulgated by the government, which are insufficient. Definite laws must be established. Moreover, to develop the Central Bank, commercial shares should be solicited, and the protection of commercial shares should be legally stipulated. As for the independence of the Central Bank, it does not mean that it is separated from financial supervision, nor is it limited to the Minister of Finance concurrently holding office. Legislation is a major national plan, focusing on laying the foundation for the Central Bank and ensuring that it can act as the national treasury and regulate finance. This is the main purpose of the recommendation of our Yuan. (9th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Ministry of Industry Plans to Establish Ammonium Sulfate Plant

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry previously sent technician Zhou Ziyue to investigate the condition of iron sulfide produced in Shuikoushan in order to establish an ammonium sulfate plant. It is heard that the investigation has been completed and that the raw materials there are very suitable for manufacturing ammonium sulfate. The factory can begin organizing this month. Comments by Arima on Way Back Home

Nagasaki - Ambassador Arima, returning home, arrived here aboard the Nagasaki Maru at 1 PM today. Once the matter is moved to the League of Nations, Japan will do its best at the League of Nations General Assembly and will decide on future actions based on how it proceeds." Foreign Important Telegrams

Roosevelt Elected President of the United States

Everyone Expected Mr. Roosevelt would Continue Hoover's Policy

Davis has been tipped to be Secretary of State

Europe Paid Close Attention and Japan expressed their good feelings

Roosevelt's Votes Created New Record in Presidential Election

Reuters, New York, 9th - At 1 AM this morning, Roosevelt was elected President of the United States to succeed Hoover. Hoover has conceded defeat.

Reuters, New York, 9th - At 1:30 AM this morning, the Republican Party appeared to be collapsing, as Roosevelt had won in 38 states, gaining a total of 434 electoral votes. Hoover only won in 6 states, gaining a total of 70 electoral votes.

Reuters, New York, 9th - Around 2 AM this morning, according to incomplete election reports, Roosevelt had gained 453 electoral votes, while Hoover only had 78.

National News Agency, New York, 9th - The count of the US presidential election votes as of approximately 2:30 AM this morning showed that Roosevelt had gained 7,765,055 votes, while Hoover only had 5,249,165 votes. Later, as of 3 AM this morning, the reported votes increased to 9,676,891 for Roosevelt and only 6,611,361 for Hoover. Calculating the repeated election votes, Roosevelt can gain 469 votes and Hoover can only gain 51 votes. Among the state votes, according to the latest reports, only four states have more votes for Hoover than for Roosevelt: Pennsylvania, Maine, New Hampshire, and Vermont.

Hoover Telegraphed Congratulations to Mr. Roosevelt

Reuters, New York, 9th - President Hoover accepted the defeat with composure and telegraphed congratulations to Roosevelt, saying, "I congratulate you on the opportunity to serve the country. I wish you success in your political career. I am willing to do my best to assist you in matters where our goals are the same."

Election "Landslide"

Reuters, New York, 9th - The number of votes obtained by Roosevelt will become a new record in presidential elections. It is expected that he will have five million more votes than the 21 million votes obtained by President Hoover in 1928. The Democratic Party has won 472 of the 531 electoral votes. Mrs. Roosevelt supports herself by editing a magazine, teaching at a girls' school, and replicating antique utensils. She usually abstains from alcohol and told Reuters reporters today that she persuaded her husband not to lift the alcohol ban too much. After receiving the report of his election, Roosevelt issued a statement to the country, saying, "I am deeply aware of the responsibility that comes with this expression of trust and will do my best to promote the welfare of the country."

Reuters, New York, 8th - The results of the election can be revealed as early as 9 PM tonight (Pacific Time). The total number of voters today is approximately 40 million.

Reuters, New York, 8th - According to the first unofficial report, Roosevelt has an advantage in seven states and has gained the support of 93 electoral districts. Hoover only has an advantage in three states, with 20 electoral districts supporting him. In Massachusetts and Pennsylvania, the number of votes for Hoover and Roosevelt is about the same. The election competition is extremely fierce in New York City and New York State. According to the first report, the number of votes obtained by Roosevelt in New York State is almost equal to that of Hoover. It is noteworthy that New York State has traditionally been the base of the Republican Party, but Roosevelt has gained more votes. As for the election in New York City, Roosevelt has an absolute majority. It is said that in this election in New York City, Roosevelt must obtain approximately 500,000 more votes than Hoover in order to suppress the Republican Party's advantage in other towns and cities.

Reuters, New York, 8th - The report received at 7 PM tonight showed that Roosevelt has an advantage in twelve states, while Hoover only has an advantage in five states. The southern states of the United States unanimously elected Roosevelt. States such as Alabama, Florida, Georgia, Oklahoma, Texas, Missouri, Maryland, Tennessee, Nebraska, Virginia, and Arkansas all unanimously lean towards Roosevelt. Roosevelt also obtained more votes than Hoover in Kansas, Massachusetts, and New York State. Hoover only obtained the support of New Hampshire, Rhode Island, Vermont, South Dakota, and Connecticut. The number of votes for the two in Pennsylvania and Colorado is the same. Generally speaking, Roosevelt has a great advantage in the election trend.

Reuters, New York, 8th - The report received at 7:30 PM tonight showed that Roosevelt has a slight advantage in New York State. In the four rural counties of the state, the number of votes for Roosevelt and Hoover is the same, but in New York City, Roosevelt obtained 400,000 more votes than Hoover.

Reuters, New York, 8th - The report received at 9:30 PM tonight proves that Roosevelt has an absolute advantage. Roosevelt has obtained the support of 25 states, with a total of 284 electoral districts voting for him. Hoover obtained more votes in seven states, with only 88 districts voting for Hoover. Roosevelt won a complete victory in the southern United States, and Hoover is showing a trend of complete collapse. If Roosevelt obtains the support of 266 electoral districts, he can be elected. Roosevelt is currently calculating the number of votes obtained with his election manager.

Glimpses of Roosevelt's Policies

Reuters, New York, 9th – Roosevelt's election may not have a significant impact on the world. American tariffs will not be greatly reduced in the future, and both parties oppose canceling war debts, only willing to reorganize them to facilitate the export of goods from debtor nations to the United States. It is expected that Roosevelt will continue Hoover's policy of limited cooperation with the League of Nations, such as in disarmament, peacemaking, and restoring the world economy. Regarding prohibition, Roosevelt may prevent the amendment of the Prohibition Act, and may show greater sympathy for unemployment issues and related relief petitions.

National News Agency, Washington, 9th – The US President-elect has been confirmed to change from Republican to Democratic, and the 73rd Congress will also be dominated by the Democratic Party. It is expected that after the new president takes office on March 4th next year, he will surely implement new policies. President-elect Roosevelt will

offer a fresh perspective. However, according to observations by political leaders here, the new initiatives of the Democratic president will first be seen in diplomatic issues and domestic affairs with international relations. Except for the prohibition issue, there may not be drastic changes. Those familiar with current affairs also anticipate that although the person in charge will change, the policies of the old government will mostly remain the same, with only slight modifications. First, regarding the Far East issue in foreign policy, President Hoover strived to oppose changes to treaty status, thus giving rise to the so-called "Open Door Policy," which advocates that in situations that endanger existing treaties, the signatory nations must consult with each other and hold meetings. This policy was tacitly endorsed in the Democratic platform. It is said that President-elect Roosevelt had been closely following Far East events even before the election campaign, and it is expected that he will not change the policies of the previous government. Furthermore, according to those close to Roosevelt, he believes that diplomatic personnel should serve long tenures and should not be replaced lightly. Therefore, it is expected that Grew will remain stationed in Tokyo, and Johnson will remain stationed in China. Second, regarding the attitude towards the League of Nations, it is said that there will be no changes, because the government will only change its attitude after public opinion changes. Recently, Peek stated at the Democratic National Convention that the United States is not prepared to join the League of Nations. This statement is sufficient to represent the Democratic Party's stance. Third, regarding disarmament policy, it is said that in practice, it will mostly remain the same, with only some party leaders hoping for more direct involvement. Therefore, if the European conference fails, the United States may take the initiative to convene a subsequent conference. Fourth, regarding the war debt issue, although Roosevelt did not express his attitude during the election campaign, it is hoped that he will show slightly more sympathy than the Republican Party for the cancellation of all or part of the debt. In addition, there will also be few changes regarding Philippine policy, because since the economic decline, the Republican Party, in order to avoid Philippine sugar and vegetable oil competing with US agricultural products, has also supported Philippine independence. Also, regarding finance, the integrity of the gold standard will continue to be maintained. The next Secretary of the Treasury will probably be Mr. Young, who drafted the Young Plan.

Incumbent President Hoover

Optimism in Geneva

Reuters, Geneva, 9th – Roosevelt's election is warmly welcomed here as a precursor to the United States showing greater sympathy for Europe's suffering and closer cooperation with the League of Nations. Davis, the US representative here, whether he returns to the United States to serve as Secretary of State or remains stationed in Europe, his reputation and views will definitely energize the work of the Disarmament Conference. As for the Manchurian problem, it is expected that the Democratic Party will not greatly change Stimson's policy.

Reuters, London, 8th – Europe is paying close attention to the US election. If Roosevelt is elected, all countries involved will pay attention to his policies on military needs, war preparedness, silver prices, and prohibition. Regarding the prohibition issue, it is believed here that if the United States implements the opening of alcohol prohibition, the profits earned by smugglers will become national taxes, which will make up for the US budget deficit.

Japan Expresses Goodwill

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 9th – Regarding the result of the US presidential election, the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs has avoided formally commenting on the election of the Democratic Party's Roosevelt as president, but the general observation is as follows: The Democratic Party, like the Republican Party, does not adopt imperialism and adheres to liberalism and coordination. Therefore, although there will be no substantial changes in its policies towards China and Japan, they may be more moderate than before. The Democratic Party is absolutely opposed to high tariffs, so Japan's trade may improve. As for the League of Nations, Roosevelt has criticized the current League of Nations, saying that it is not in line with Wilson's spirit, and may not be as close as Hoover. However, Stimson will come out and be active in the League of Nations General Assembly. Because he lost the election, he may not have an active attitude, which is more beneficial to Japan.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 9th – Because of the Manchurian issue and tariff issues, the financial community in Japan, which has been suppressed by the Republican Party, is very welcoming of the election of Democratic candidate Roosevelt as president. The liberalism of international coordination and tariff reduction advocated by the Democratic Party will also have a good impact on Japan, so the future of raw silk consumption is optimistic. In particular, if the independence of the Philippines is realized, it is believed that it will have a better impact on Japan-US trade.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 9th – Because the Democratic Party's Roosevelt was elected US President, the morale in all Japanese markets has become active, and market prices have risen. For example, the opening transaction price of the raw silk clearing market broke through 100 yen. Although the closing price fell, it stopped at 100 yen, and the stock market also soared.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 9th – Regarding the election of the Democratic Party's Roosevelt as President of the United States, the Governor of the Bank of Japan, Mr. Hisato, said that Roosevelt's election as President is not surprising. However, important issues such as the League of Nations' attitude towards the Manchurian problem, the World Economic Conference, and the war debt problem have all been temporarily suspended due to this election. Regardless of who is elected, from an international perspective, the end of the election is a good thing. The United States itself will be liberated from the election fever and return to normal, and will calmly study ways to resolve the world's panic. Although it is not known who will be the next Secretary of State, on the Manchurian issue, they will not adopt the stimulating attitude of today. The world's diplomatic circles will take Japan as the center to see the light. As a result, the Japanese financial world in general may be positively affected.

Reasons for Hoover's Failure

Reuters, New York, 9th – There are two reasons why President Hoover was not re-elected. One is the blind hatred of millions of Americans who are experiencing difficult times, and the other is that the Republican Party's propaganda and arrangements were not as perfect as the Democratic Party's. President Hoover's doubtful attitude towards prohibition also caused those in the same party who advocated for the relaxation of the ban to no longer support him. This is also one of the reasons why President Hoover was unable to be re-elected.

A Brief Biography of Roosevelt

Roosevelt was born on January 30, 1882, in Hyde Park, New York. As a child, he was taught by French and German governesses. At the age of fourteen, he entered Groton School. He enjoyed outdoor sports. In 1904, he graduated from Harvard University. The 26th President of the United States, Theodore Roosevelt, was his cousin. After the Spanish-American War, the United States actively promoted the navy, so he had a keen interest in naval issues. In 1905, he married Miss Anna. In 1907, he engaged in legal practice and had a special interest in naval cases. In 1910, he entered politics and was elected as a Democratic state legislator in his hometown. Later, he opposed the Tammany Hall faction, which caused a huge wave in the Democratic Party, and he gained fame for this. In 1913, he was elected to a consecutive term as a New York State legislator, but was also appointed as Assistant Secretary of the Navy. Therefore, he had to resign from his position as a legislator and take up the position of Assistant Secretary of the Navy, which was close to his aspirations. The period during which he held this position was the time when the European War broke out, which allowed him to further develop his research on the navy and implement his advocacy for expanding naval armaments. He also dared to independently issue huge emergency military expenditures before Congress formally passed the military budget, and devoted his full efforts to seeking naval victory in the European War. He attended the Versailles Conference and had a good impression and affection for the League of Nations. From 1913 to 1920, he served as Assistant Secretary of the Navy for eight years. In the 1920 presidential election, he was nominated as the Democratic candidate for president. He delivered 1,000 campaign speeches, but ultimately lost to Harding and Coolidge. After the election defeat, he returned to his legal practice. In 1921, Roosevelt, who was already forty years old, was still in good health, but after the election defeat, he expressed a negative attitude because he no longer advocated naval competition, but instead advocated a naval holiday. In the winter of 1921, he went to Campo Bello Island for rest. He caught a cold from swimming in cold water, and after a sickness, he lost his health. His legs became numb and his movements became inconvenient, and he has not recovered to this day. In 1928, he made great efforts for Smith's presidential candidacy. Due to Smith's repeated urging, he came out and ran for Governor of New York State, and served until he retired in 1931. Since running for Governor of New York, all Democrats in the United States have admired his campaigning abilities. On July 1 of this year, he was nominated as the Democratic candidate for president. Today, he was elected as the President of the United States with a large majority.

Japan's Large-Scale Military Expansion

Yesterday's Cabinet Meeting Decided to Restore Allocations

Military Spending Will Increase by 56 Million Yuan

Naval Expansion Costs 460 Million Yuan

Issuance of Public Bonds Increased by 50 Million Yen

Reuters, Tokyo, 9th – According to the Japanese newspaper, the Ministry of the Navy has decided to quickly carry out its second naval replenishment plan and will ask the Diet to approve the necessary funds, which are estimated to cost 460 million Japanese yen. The funds will be appropriated over four years starting from the 1933-34 fiscal year. The naval replenishment plan includes two 8,500-ton cruisers, seven 1,400-ton destroyers, one 8,000-ton aircraft carrier, six submarines of various types, one minelayer, and some minesweepers and torpedo boats. The above projects will cost 360 million yuan, and the remaining 100 million yuan will be used to add five naval air squadrons. At that time, Japan will have more than 36 air squadrons. According to the Japanese newspaper, the Ministry of the Navy does not acknowledge this statement, but also does not deny that it is completely unfounded. Therefore, the public believes that this statement is not entirely without cause.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 9th – Regarding the Ministry of Finance's review of the requests for restoration by various ministries, out of the total amount of 285 million yuan including 130 million yuan from the Army Ministry, 60 million yuan from the Navy Ministry, 40 million yuan from the Ministry of Interior, and 20 million yuan from the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry, only 32 million yuan were approved by the Ministry of Finance. How this will be allocated is of great concern. As a result of yesterday's meeting of the Ministry of Finance, it was decided that the amount of the restoration request would be limited to a total of 32 million yuan, most of which would be used for military spending. How military spending and other expenditures outside of it will be allocated will be decided by today's Cabinet meeting. Because the Ministry of Finance and the military ministers are in political conflict over how to allocate the above-mentioned amount in the Army and Navy's restoration requests, today's Cabinet meeting only decided on the general outline of how to allocate the 32 million yuan, which includes the military spending in the original budget. A decision must be made after the military exercises.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 9th – The Army Ministry held a meeting yesterday to further discuss the restoration requests, all of which stated that there was no room for further reduction after several cuts. The Director of the Accounting Bureau, Mr. Onodera, visited the Director of the Budget Bureau, Mr. Fujii, at the Ministry of Finance yesterday afternoon, requesting the restoration of 130 million yuan, which included 60 million yuan for military equipment improvement costs and 70 million yuan for Manchurian incident costs. Mr. Fujii refused to approve it because he believed that the request was too large. The practical negotiations failed at this point. However, the Army Ministry stated that although 60 million yuan for military equipment improvement costs and a part of the Manchurian incident costs must be included in the budget, most of the Manchurian incident costs can be kept as reserve funds by the Ministry of Finance with a slightly wider amount. If the Ministry of Finance insists on limiting the issuance of public bonds to 800 million yuan, it will not be able to fulfill the mission of the military. Since the Ministry of Finance and the military have different views, the Minister of Finance, Mr. Takahashi, and the Minister of the Army, Mr. Araki, will have to resolve the issue politically, either in the form of an additional budget or by frankly admitting the restoration. In short, there is no other way but to increase the issuance of public bonds. As a result, public bonds may be increased by 50 to 60 million yuan.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo – At 11:00 AM today, an extraordinary cabinet meeting was held at the Prime Minister's official residence. Prime Minister Saito and all cabinet members attended. Finance Minister Takahashi said that he had conducted practical negotiations with various ministries regarding the restoration requests that had been reduced in next year's budget, but the results had not yet reached the stage of reporting. The proposed amount of restoration approval is limited to within 32 million Japanese yen. As for the military equipment improvement costs of the Army and Navy, negotiations are still underway with the military ministers. The above-mentioned 32 million Japanese yen is to increase the reserve funds for the Manchurian Incident costs, and the restoration of the various ministries will be left to the Finance Minister to handle. The ministers continued to express their opinions on the desired restoration. As a result, the reserve funds for the Manchurian Incident costs were increased by 10 million Japanese yen, and the remaining 22 million Japanese yen was allocated to various ministries.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo – After today's extraordinary cabinet meeting, Finance Minister Takahashi held political negotiations with Army Minister Araki and Navy Minister Okada regarding the reduction of military equipment improvement costs. As a result, the negotiations were generally completed. The content has not yet been released. However, it seems that the limit for the issuance of public bonds has been increased by 50 million yen to cover the military's restoration requests. Out of the limit of 32 million Japanese yen for approving the restoration requests, 10 million Japanese yen will be added to the Manchurian Incident costs, and the remaining 22 million will be allocated to various ministries. The final decision on this negotiation will be made today or tomorrow.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo – Following today's cabinet meeting, Prime Minister Saito, Finance Minister Takahashi, Army Minister Araki, and Navy Minister Okada stayed behind to consult on the Army and Navy's restoration requests. As a result, a satisfactory solution was reached as follows: 1. In addition to the 10 million Japanese yen in the initially set reserve funds for the Manchurian Incident costs, an additional 10 million Japanese yen was approved for restoration. 2. The restoration requests of the various ministries will be supplemented with the remaining 22 million Japanese yen. 3. The total amount of the restoration requests for military equipment improvement costs is 90 million Japanese yen. The financial resources for this will be an increase in the issuance of public bonds. As a result, the Director of the Accounting Bureau of the Ministry of the Navy, Mr. Kato, visited the Director of the Accounting Bureau of the Ministry of the Army, Mr. Onodera, at 4:30 PM to negotiate the allocation of the 90 million yen. As a result, it was decided that the Army would receive 65 million yen and the Navy would receive 25 million yen. The Army and Navy authorities will base this on the settlement of accounts today and submit the budget proposal to the Ministry of Finance.

Stalemate in Japan-Russia Negotiations

The Two Governments' Opinions Differ

Matsuoka Departed from Warsaw to Geneva

Reuters, Warsaw, 9th – Japanese representative Matsuoka and others arrived here from Moscow last night. Today, they visited government officials and departed for Geneva in the evening.

Reuters, Tokyo, 9th – The Ministry of Foreign Affairs received a telegram from Moscow reporting that Matsuoka's conversation with the Soviet authorities showed that the Soviet government believed that the Russo-Japanese non-aggression treaty and the Soviet Union's recognition of "Manchukuo" were mutually related. Therefore, it cannot agree to one and abandon the other. A spokesperson for the Ministry of Foreign Affairs commented on this today, saying that the Japanese government's opinion is that the two matters are completely unrelated. Therefore, the Soviet Union's recognition of "Manchukuo" should not be a condition for concluding a non-aggression treaty, as the conclusion of this treaty should be judged on its own merits and has nothing to do with external affairs.
