Anglo-American Prevention of Japanese Goods Dumping

Imposing High Tariffs

Osaka Mainichi Newspaper reports that the Assistant Secretary of the Customs Bureau of the US Treasury Department, Mr. Dawe, issued a dumping evaluation on the 3rd for goods such as tuna, salmon, and electric bulbs imported from Japan, instructing customs officials to complete the investigation and at the same time instructing each customs to prohibit the import of Japanese goods. However, according to Mr. Dawe's statement, the import of Japanese goods has almost been prevented. In the Philippines, there is also a deep concern about the sharp drop in yen prices (Japanese-US exchange rate), and Japanese goods will inevitably be dumped in the port. Therefore, the Philippine Congress has, in accordance with the proposal of Governor Roosevelt, stipulated that tariffs on the import of Japanese goods should be levied in gold, which is also to prevent their import.

According to Kokumin Shimbun, the Japanese Chargé d'Affaires in the United States, Mr. Saito, reported that US manufacturers held a large public hearing from October 19th to 25th to discuss the problem of repelling Japanese goods. The resolution was to petition the government, stating that domestic factories producing matches, marine products, ceramics, electric bulbs, carpets, and other miscellaneous goods have closed down one after another due to the pressure from Japanese goods, and workers are unemployed. They requested that the authorities impose high tariffs and prohibit unfair low-price competition. Recently, President Hoover traveled around various places for the election issue, warning the people to pay attention to the threat of Japanese goods. Along the Pacific coast, the American fishing industry is facing a crisis, and the vegetable canning industry, food industry, bean industry, copper and iron industries, etc., are also declining day by day. They oppose the Democratic Party's low tariff policy and advocate imposing high tariffs on Japanese goods. Also, Conservative Party member John in the British House of Commons believes that the dumping of Japanese goods affects the silk weaving industry and strongly advocates suppressing it. The current British Chancellor of the Exchequer has ordered the Customs Advisory Committee to investigate the tariffs on Japanese silk fabrics. On the one hand, British silk fabric manufacturers are about to petition the Customs Advisory Committee. At the same time, Conservative Party member Levy has proposed a bill to prevent the import of Japanese goods to the UK and American territories, urging the government to quickly study countermeasures to avoid the bankruptcy of the industrial community.

British Parliament Ends Discussion on Unemployment Relief Issues

Many Suggestions from Various Parties

Still No Concrete Solution

Reuters, London, 8th – The three-day debate on the unemployment issue in the House of Commons ended today with a final speech by Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain. Many suggestions were put forward by various parties during the debate. The Conservative Party mostly advocated preferential treatment for farmers, and Lloyd George and others advocated developing small land ownership systems. Former Chancellor of the Exchequer Horne of the Conservative Party spoke about prices and the position of gold and silver, saying that wholesale prices could be raised by restricting the supply of goods or changing the amount of gold coins. Some countries hoarding cash have led to a gold shortage, so the British may as well use silver to supplement the lack of gold. If silver prices rise, then the trade between Britain and China and India will greatly improve. If the international exchange rate is set to normal, it will be even more beneficial to world industry and commerce. The world has nothing more than a large amount of cash, but about three-quarters of it is held in the hands of two countries, so other countries do not have the necessary supply. This kind of problem is one of the major causes of the current situation. Today, the price of British currency is equal to the time when the United States first announced the cancellation of the gold standard, and the purchasing power of the pound in terms of goods is greater than it was five years ago. This is sufficient evidence that people do not need to worry about the depreciation of the pound. If silver is used in the appropriate position relative to the world's monetary system, industry and commerce can benefit more than any plan. Horne advocated that the state should subsidize the Cunard Shipping Company to carry out its plan to build two large merchant ships to provide jobs for the unemployed, and also advocated quickly abolishing the order prohibiting borrowing. Former Home Secretary Samuel hoped that the upcoming World Economic Conference would have the opportunity to resolve issues such as tax rates and monetary systems. This is necessary to restore prosperity and end unemployment. If the Disarmament Conference can have satisfactory results at the same time, then there will be enough courage to encourage the whole world to improve the economic situation.

Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain stood up to conclude the debate, saying that he found it difficult to accept the idea that raising silver prices could promote trade between Britain and China and India. China uses silver coins, while India does not. Therefore, as far as India is concerned, this statement should be based on the premise that the value of the silver stored by Indians is high, and India's trade with other countries can be expanded. Most of the silver stored in India is not for silver coins, but for silver ornaments. India used to store silver not as a medium for shopping, but as a sign of its wealth. In recent years, changes in silver prices have not been found in India's import figures. There is evidence that Indians use their hoarded silver to buy more goods from other countries when silver prices rise. As for China, the situation is slightly different. China uses silver. When silver prices are high, its currency value rises and its purchasing power is also strong, but its sales power decreases. An examination of China's import figures also does not show equal differences due to changes in silver prices. During the period when silver prices fell by 27 percent, China's imports only fell by 10 percent. He did not see that high silver prices could have much effect on the trade of Lancashire cotton with China and India. As for increasing the supply of hard goods to promote world wholesale prices, it should be known that the supply of gold has already increased greatly. In 1900, it was worth 1 billion pounds in English gold, and this year it has increased to 2.5 billion pounds. The discovery of gold mines in California and Australia in the 19th century and the development of gold mines in Africa thereafter meant that the supply of cash was greater than before. Gold coins were greatly affected, but since the number of increases has already been two and a half times in the past thirty years, even if large gold mines are discovered in the future, they may not have the same impact on the amount required for coinage. It has now been proposed that central banks should agree to accept some silver in proportion to gold at a certain ratio, and that this silver price should be the market price. If this is the case, then the market price will not be able to induce India and China to release their hoarded silver. China needs silver as currency, and silver does not come from China unless silver prices are high and China needs less silver. If silver prices rise to two shillings and there are 100 million ounces of the highest amount of silver, this is only an increase equal to 100 million pounds of gold in the supply of 2.5 billion pounds of gold. This kind of auxiliary supply is only about 2 percent, which is too small to have a significant effect. Therefore, he believes that using silver to help gold may not be beneficial in the current environment, and the central banks of various countries may not all agree to use this system. He did not make any compound currency proposals that could solve our difficulties. After the Chancellor of the Exchequer's speech, the House of Commons passed the Labour Party's motion, expressing Congress's anxiety about the unemployed and welcoming various relief methods.

Zheng Tianxi to Inspect Judicial Conditions in Various Places

The Ministry of Justice, in order to investigate the judicial conditions throughout the country as a reference for practical policy guidelines, must have the minister personally inspect at the end of each year. This year, Minister Luo is unable to leave Beijing due to business and sent Vice Minister Zheng Tianxi as his representative. It was originally scheduled to depart within days, but the judge's preliminary examination has not yet been announced and must be postponed for five or six days before departure. In addition to Vice Minister Zheng, Zhu Yutang and Ling Shijun were also hired as inspectors. Zhu has been working in the legal field for many years and has served as a judge of the Dali Temple and the head of the high courts in Jiangxi and other provinces. Ling is also a judicial elder and has served as the president of the high court. Both have extremely rich experience and knowledge and can be competent for this important task. Zheng and the other three each divided the region and took their staff to inspect the districts separately. Zheng inspected Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, and other provinces. Zhu inspected Shandong, Shanxi, Beiping, Tianjin, Chahar, and other places in North China. Ling inspected Jiangxi, Hunan, Hubei, Anhui, and other provinces in Central China. Ling and Zhu will be able to depart in two or three days. The scope of the inspection was determined by the inspectors after days of consultation and the drafting of outlines. The general system is to inspect the courts, prisons, the adjudication system of each county, and the prisons of each county, paying attention to their work spirit and how to eliminate accumulated malpractices. The focus is on the judicial situation in each county today. The county governments in China also handle judicial affairs, and the general situation is mostly due to the old habits and accumulated malpractices. Therefore, the ministry should find ways to improve so that it can be slightly beneficial to the people in practical terms. It is heard that the inspection period will take about two or three months to complete.

Judicial Yuan Interprets Legal Issues

The Judicial Yuan's Unified Interpretation of Laws and Regulations Conference recently resolved to interpret three items of legal ambiguity, which are recorded separately as follows:

Temple Management: If a temple with a resident abbot was built or repaired by the abbot through donations, whether the temple should be abolished or not, its property is public property and not official property. (The standard for the existence or abolition of shrines is a matter of the existence or abolition of shrines, and has nothing to do with temple property.) It must not be allocated by local government offices to any group, and no local group may occupy or demolish it without authorization. If a temple with a resident monk or Taoist priest is dilapidated and can be considered abandoned, it should be handled in accordance with Article 4 of the Regulations on Supervising Temples. If there is no resident monk or Taoist priest, if it is a temporary state, the church to which it belongs or the competent government office should solicit the opinions of the monks and Taoists of the same religion in the local area and select a resident priest to manage it. Local groups must not occupy or demolish it.

Female Inheritance: If the property that a married woman should inherit has already been distributed by other heirs, according to the provisions of Article 3 of the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of Retroactive Inheritance of Property, if her request for re-distribution is made more than six months after the implementation of the detailed rules, it should not be approved regardless of whether the distribution is appropriate. If it is after the implementation of the Inheritance Compilation of the Civil Code, it should be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 3 of the Implementation Law of the Compilation.

Inland River Vessels: If a vessel can only navigate inland rivers, even if its gross tonnage exceeds the limit shown in Article 2, Paragraph 1 of the Maritime Law, it is not applicable to the Maritime Law because its nature is different from that of the vessels stipulated in Article 1.

Truth About the Guangdong Air Force Accident

Ye Xiasheng Petitions Chen Jitang to Honor His Son

Guangzhou Correspondence - The truth about the Guangdong Air Force accident caused by testing the on-board radio with land communication is described in detail in a document submitted by Ye Daguan's father, Ye Xiasheng, to Chen Jitang. The document reads: "Submitting a petition for my son, Ye Daguan, who sacrificed his life for science and his ambition was not fulfilled, I pour out the true facts of what happened, pleading for a clear order of commendation to complete his legacy, to inspire and encourage future generations to strengthen the military and consolidate national defense. My eldest son, Ye Daguan, is twenty-one years old this year. Because I was traveling in all directions, he repeatedly lost his education. He only began studying in the junior class of Beiping Chengda Middle School at the age of fifteen. From then on, he followed me north and south, and the seats were not warm. In the autumn of the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, when I was serving in the Northern Expeditionary Army, my son saw a military shortwave radio and began to study it, feeling that it was very interesting. So he closed the door and studied on his own, exploring the source and tracing the root. In less than a month, he was able to make a radio receiver from copper and iron without seeking external help. After a year, he returned to Guangdong and continued his research. He then served in the Materials Department of the Radio Bureau of the Ministry of Military Affairs. Fortunately, there were no mistakes for many years. Later, due to changes in the bureau's affairs, he resigned and returned home to study engineering school to make up for English calculations. Because of his diligent and tireless nature, he always burned the midnight oil, forgot to eat and sleep, did not take off his clothes until a lesson was finished, and did not set foot on the country until a plan was completed. He took saving the country with science as his duty every day and sacrificing himself for science as his purpose at all times. Since the January 28th Sino-Japanese War this year, he learned that the captured enemy planes seemed to have an aerial radio device, so he was able to detect intelligence and command easily. He then took it upon himself to invent this radio telephone. At first, he faced the wall for three months, as if he were a wooden chicken. Then, he threw up his sleeves and stood up, boasting that he had succeeded. I thought his ambition was commendable and gave him my support. The total amount was more than ten thousand yuan. In the autumn of this year, the Air Force learned of his ability and ordered him to go to the department for testing. From September 19th to October 21st, when the accident occurred, there were more than twenty tests. He was deeply praised by Commander Huang and Chief of Staff Lin, who believed that the results were remarkable and better than those of foreigners. Commander Huang also inquired and commended him, intending to award him a middle-level official position. My son declined because he was young and ignorant and wanted to study further. However, he still worked hard and diligently, without any thought of power or profit, and was sincere in defending the country from beginning to end. He never asked for a single penny and never hoped for a little vanity. His sincerity was already seen by Commander Huang and Chief of Staff Lin and has already been reported. I humbly hope that the accident in which my son was killed was caused by what reason, since the two people on board died at the same time, there is no way to stand up and testify. However, according to the investigation, my son had achieved excellent results in repeated tests and was not a novice trying for the first time. The three abalone bolts inside the engine of the destroyed telephone, the large and small rubber wires, were not melted, which does not seem to be caused by the telephone. My son's clothes and skin had no traces of electricity, which can be used to confirm. Now that the deceased is gone, why should I argue about merits and demerits? Even if I argue, what practical benefit is there? However, I remember that my son's aerial radio telephone, which was tested and effective, is of great importance to military and national defense. This achievement should not be covered up by a single flaw, and your generosity in encouraging the new aircraft and guiding the latecomers will surely not stop eating because of a hot soup. Therefore, I propose that Your Excellency investigate and verify the test results of my son's invention of the aerial radio telephone, issue a clear order of commendation, and order the Air Force Command to quickly select talented people to improve and continue to complete my son's unfinished legacy, to inspire and encourage future generations to strengthen the military and consolidate national defense. Then, even if my son dies, he should be grateful for the great virtue in the nine springs. Sincerely presented to Chen, Commander-in-Chief of the First Army Group."

Yesterday, it sent letters to the provincial capital Public Security Bureau, Highway Administration Bureau, and military and police inspection offices and other agencies, and scheduled a discussion on the deployment and planning of winter defense at the Provincial Government Security Office on the afternoon of the 10th.

Head of the Department of Civil Affairs Returns to Province After Inspection Tour - Lv Bichou, head of the Department of Civil Affairs of Zhejiang, went to Ning, Shao, Wen, and Tai in eastern Zhejiang last month to investigate politics and local customs. He has been traveling for more than a month. Lv returned to the province from Wenling yesterday and went to the provincial government to visit Chairman Lu's illness. Today (the 9th), he took his own car to Beijing on the national highway to report to the Executive Yuan on the situation of his tour to various counties.

Ningbo

Four Families Robbed in One Night in Qianxu Village - Qianxu Village in eastern Yin is densely populated and commercially prosperous. On the evening of the previous day (the 6th) at about 12 pm, five or six bandits armed with weapons first broke into Li Qiantai's pickled goods store and robbed more than 100 yuan in silver dollars. They then went to the Yongxing meat shop next door and robbed more than 100 yuan in silver dollars and gold jewelry worth about 200 yuan. They then broke into the Caishun cake shop and robbed 19 yuan in silver dollars. Finally, they went to the Yufeng rice shop and robbed about 200 yuan.

Shaoxing

Punishing Traitors Sparks Repercussions: Hang Da Sheng Cloth Shop in Qingfeng Lane, Shaoxing, recently received a large shipment of cloth from Shanghai, all of which was counterfeit Japanese goods. The Shaoxing Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association was notified via a confidential telegram from Shanghai. On the afternoon of the 7th, they dispatched an inspection team to the shop and other cloth shops for inspection. Hang Da Sheng claimed that the cloth was of British brand and refused inspection. The two sides argued, and the iron gates were closed, arousing suspicion among the inspection team members, who intensified the inspection. Eight large boxes, totaling more than 430 pieces, of counterfeit Shanghai Lun Chang and Wujin Dyeing and Weaving Factory Japanese goods were found on the spot. The Anti-Japanese Association sealed them and stored them at the county government. On the morning of the 8th, the association, believing that Hang Da Sheng Cloth Shop was secretly hiding a large number of Japanese goods and dared to resist by closing its doors and inciting a crowd, intentionally disrupting the national salvation work, convened a meeting of representatives from various legal entities. They decided to have the shop's person in charge, Shen Ji Ren, stand in a wooden cage according to the method of punishing traitors. A Mr. Zhou, who resisted on behalf of the shop, was paraded through the streets. The shop was sealed and will remain closed until the case is resolved. After the meeting, the decisions were implemented separately. The traitorous merchant Shen Ji Sheng was paraded through the streets and stood in a wooden cage for two hours before being sent to the Public Security Bureau for detention, leading to a city-wide strike by all cloth shops to support Da Sheng. Outside their doors, they wrote: "All employees of this shop support Da Sheng. Employees voluntarily suspend business to support Da Sheng." Da Sheng's employees went to the county government to petition.

38 Professors at Beiping Normal University Oppose Changes to the School System

Jiangsu Education Department Compiles Secondary School Curriculum Schedule

Based on Ministry-Promulgated Curriculum Standards

Detailed Schedule Catalog Developed

The Jiangsu Education Department, in order to improve the level of secondary schools, previously promulgated a plan to raise the level of secondary schools. Now, in view of the fact that the curriculum progress of various schools is often uneven and the levels inevitably vary, a committee was organized to hire experts to develop a detailed schedule catalog based on the Ministry-promulgated standards. Each week and each hour are specifically regulated so that both teaching parties have adequate preparation, so that the progress will not be uneven and the courses to be studied will be completed on schedule, which is the best way to improve the level. The department has drafted a budget and submitted it to the provincial government for approval. Here is an excerpt of the proposal:

Jiangsu is reorganizing education throughout the province and effectively improving the level of secondary schools. Since the 21st year of the Republic, graduation examinations have been held, and all facilities have been promulgated and implemented in order. However, graduation examinations can only determine the level of teaching performance of each school. In order to ensure that regular teaching is effective and progress is balanced, a temporary examination by the graduation examination is not enough. The Ministry of Education promulgated the Secondary School Curriculum Standards for trial implementation, and the provinces and cities reported separately, and the Ministry convened experts to revise them in detail. It is reported that the amendments have been promulgated in order. The department will implement the above curriculum standards to give secondary schools throughout the province the opportunity to innovate teaching and science. The standards issued by the Ministry only list the outlines. For practical implementation, detailed items must be compiled. It is urgent to examine the actual situation in the province based on the standards issued by the Ministry, and invite experts in social science and natural science in the province with experience in secondary education to jointly study and compile the progress of each subject's courses, and distribute them so that the teaching materials in secondary schools throughout the province are appropriate and the level is uniform. For all high school subjects such as civics, Chinese, English, arithmetic, zoology, botany, physics, chemistry, national history, foreign history, national geography, foreign geography, health, mineralogy, and ethics, a total of fifteen subjects. For junior high school subjects such as civics, Chinese, English, arithmetic, natural history, geography, and health, a total of eight subjects. Depending on the complexity of the courses, two committee members will be hired for complex subjects, and one for simpler ones. The temporary quota is 30 people. It is planned to convene a meeting during the winter vacation of this year, and the results of the research will be prepared for printing and distribution to various schools as a standard for implementation in the next semester. However, this matter is cumbersome, and the hired committee members must be specifically responsible. The estimated remuneration is at least 200 yuan per person, which totals 6,000 yuan for 30 people, and the costs of hospitality and printing are not included. This expense is not included in the department's budget. It is proposed to pass it to the Department of Finance to be paid from the provincial reserve fund so that it can be allocated at the time. Is it appropriate? Please decide.

The Annual Meeting of the China Child Education Society to Open Tomorrow in Beijing

The third annual meeting of the China Child Education Society will be held in Beijing at 9:00 am on the 11th. The annual meeting schedule, etc., has been recorded in this newspaper. The latest news from the association is recorded below.

A Short History of the General Assembly

In the autumn of the 15th year of the Republic, comrades in Beijing and Shanghai who studied early childhood education, in view of the importance of early childhood education and the lack of research institutions and related publications in China, in December of that year, united with comrades from the Gulou Kindergarten to organize the Early Childhood Education Research Association and publish the Early Childhood Education Monthly and the Early Childhood Education Series to discuss and study practical issues in early childhood education. This was the beginning of the association. In March of the 16th year of the Republic, more comrades in the domestic education community joined the research. In order to expand the scope, it was renamed the Child Education Society. At the same time, the Early Childhood Education Monthly was renamed the Child Education Monthly. In July of the 18th year of the Republic, education comrades from Beijing, Shanghai, Hangzhou, and Beiping, Guangzhou and other places joined the research in increasing numbers. In July of the same year, a formal establishment meeting was held in Hangzhou, stipulating eight articles of association, deciding that the society would be a purely academic research institution, and that the purpose of the society was to study primary school education, early childhood education, family education, focus on practical educational problems, and provide concrete teaching materials. The society is now located at No. 50 Beijing Road. Branches have been added in major cities such as Nanjing one after another. There are more than 30 agency group members and more than 700 individual members distributed in Nanjing, Shanghai, Wuxi, Zhenjiang, Beiping, Hangzhou, Guangzhou, Fuzhou, Jinan, Anqing, Wuhu and other places. The second annual meeting was held in Shanghai. This year's second annual meeting will be held in Beijing.

Jinan Education Bureau Sends a Commissioner to Participate

Prior to the annual meeting, letters were sent to various agencies inviting them to attend and provide guidance. Institutions such as the Ministry of Education, Beijing Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, and the Department of Education of Central University all sent personnel to participate. The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau was also invited. Director Pan has always attached great importance to the study of child education. As he was busy with other matters and unable to attend in person, he appointed Hu Shuyi, a commissioner of the bureau, to represent him. It is reported that Mr. Hu left for Beijing yesterday.

Appeal by Teachers and Staff in Hubei Province After Resigning

Six Months and Ninety Percent in Arrears | Running Around and Appealing Yields No Results

Hankou, 7th Correspondence: All teachers and staff of Hubei Provincial schools and museums, due to the lack of payment and difficult living conditions, recently submitted a general resignation. All levels of schools were thus effectively on strike, and tens of thousands of young people suddenly lost their schooling. All teachers and staff telegraphed General Commander Chiang on the 4th, requesting prompt relief. The telegram read: "General Commander Chiang Junjian: Hubei education funds are six months and ninety percent in arrears. Running around and appealing has yielded no results. Recently, the provincial government's decision on education funding cannot reflect your concern for education and the actual lives of teachers and staff. Teachers and staff are unable to support themselves and are suffering from hunger and cold. They have no choice but to resign to the heads of various schools and museums. They respectfully request that the competent authorities be ordered to provide prompt relief, with deep gratitude. All teachers and staff of Hubei Provincial schools and museums kowtow in support." A declaration was also issued, stating the reasons for the resignation. The original text is as follows: "All circles should be aware that Hubei has unfortunately suffered from banditry and natural disasters in recent years, leading to economic bankruptcy and a failure to repair the administration. The impact on education is particularly significant. Since last year, education funding has been in arrears, especially much. As of now, four tenths of the December salary of last year, and all of January, February, March, August, and September of this year, and five tenths of July, are owed, for a total of six months and ninety percent of salaries. This is an unprecedented record in the education sector. In this situation, Hubei education has long been unsustainable, but teachers and staff are still enduring hunger and cold, trying to support it, adhering to the meaning of sharing difficulties and not wanting to see the education that is the lifeline of the country suddenly interrupted. They also hope that the government will have relief measures to solve the crisis. Unexpectedly, it has been delayed until now and there is still no result. The so-called clearing of salaries owed before April with the 21st year of the Republic's rehabilitation public bonds is just the face value of an unrealized bond. The so-called allocation of half of the newly added business tax is entirely for the salaries owed after July to the teachers and staff who were laid off this time, which is an empty principle with no fixed date or amount, and the reissuance of salaries to those who remain employed is still far off. The monthly salaries of teachers and staff were already meager, especially since February of this year, when they have been repeatedly reduced. Even if they were fully paid on schedule according to the cost of living in Wuhan, it would still be difficult to maintain. Now, even this small amount is unavailable. Their plight can be imagined. Moreover, since the four rural areas have been unstable in recent years, there is no peace of mind. Even if the teachers and staff themselves are willing to serve the public with empty stomachs, what about their parents and wives crying from hunger and cold? If they abandoned their parents and wives, it would not only be difficult for the teachers and staff to feel at ease, but it would also be against human nature. In the past six months, some teachers and staff have been evicted for defaulting on rent, some have been crying in their cold clothes because they have no way to cook, and some have died without medical care or burial expenses. As for borrowing and mortgaging, it has become a more common phenomenon. Recently, they have mortgaged everything and exhausted all means of borrowing. Therefore, the teachers and staff's request for the payment of arrears is driven by the pressure of life and the desire to clear debts and relieve accumulated difficulties, and is by no means a purely creditor-debtor issue with the government. If the government's current method of solving education funding is followed, it will not help the actual difficulties of teachers and staff at all. The teachers and staff, at a meeting of all representatives on November 1, decided to resign to the heads of various schools and museums to seek other livelihoods. At a time when the country is in great difficulty, all compatriots should endure hardships and share difficulties. However, a careful examination of the facts is not entirely the same as other institutions. The salaries of the personnel of many agencies were paid up to September, and the salaries owed to the laid-off personnel were also paid in one lump sum (this is the case with the Education Department). The same are citizens, the same serve society, and the same are subject to the jurisdiction of a government, but the treatment is different. What would their feelings be if they were in each other's shoes? What is even more puzzling to the teachers and staff is that the Education Department, as the highest administrative organ for education in the province, bears the heavy responsibility of raising education funding. However, it has always been perfunctory and has never provided any relief measures. If the teachers and staff make any requests, they are either delegated to the provincial government or the General Headquarters, as if the establishment of the Education Department is only for show. This has greatly disappointed the teachers and staff. Education is the foundation of the nation. This is true in Europe and the United States, and the late Premier Sun's founding program clearly stipulates guaranteeing independent education funding and raising teachers' salaries. However, Hubei's education funding has not only been in arrears until July, but it has also been repeatedly reduced. In reality, the salaries received are less than those of the clerks and recorders in various agencies. This not only affects the lives of teachers and staff, but also seriously violates the late Premier's will and hinders the development of the country's future. This is another issue that must be appealed sincerely, hoping that society will pay attention. In short, all teachers and staff have received considerable education and are not ignorant of their responsibilities to the country and society. If they are able to do so, they are willing to make every effort and will never betray their conscience and make excessive demands to belittle human relationships. This resignation is truly a last resort. Teachers and staff are not only pained by the bankruptcy of education, but also feel the lack of livelihood. Both public and private matters are plagued and anxious. They earnestly plead for understanding and assistance.

The association's funding shall be provided by the following items." I have received your query, and I hereby inform you that I have received your order, and I hereby order you to inform you and comply with it. I hereby issue this order to inform you and comply with it separately.

Yesterday's Football Match: Tung Wah Wins Against British Navy

Result: 7 to 1

Yesterday, the Tung Wah football team defeated the British Navy team with a score of 7-1 at the baseball field. This was a friendly match. The following is a record of the events:

The strength of the Connaught team was mediocre. Tung Wah originally planned to play a mixed team of the Army and Navy yesterday, but due to the short notice, they were unable to arrange it. Instead, the Connaught team from the Navy played. This team's strength was mediocre and could not withstand the strong Tung Wah team, resulting in a one-sided game with few highlights.

Li Yichen Opens the Score. The game started at 3:00 PM. The Navy kicked off and launched a spirited attack directly into Tung Wah's territory. After multiple attacks, Lu Zhongen defused the danger. Wan Xianghua attacked on the left, but lacked support in the center, making his efforts futile. Soon, Chen Jiaqiu dribbled the ball past two defenders and passed it in front of the goal. The goalkeeper rushed out to save the ball, but Li Yichen took the initiative, hitting the goalkeeper with the ball, which bounced back to Feng Yunyou in front of the goal. The goalkeeper had not yet returned, and Yichen shot into the empty goal, successfully opening the scoring.

Jiaqiu and Yichen Score Again. After the kickoff, in less than three minutes, Tu Kaiyuan threw the ball from the left sideline. Chen Hongguang passed it to Wan Xianghua on the left, who ran forward and crossed the ball directly in front of the goal. The goalkeeper caught it but fumbled, and Jiaqiu charged up and kicked the ball into the net. The goalkeeper panicked and was helpless. Afterwards, Li Yichen received a pass from Hongguang and scored another goal towards the left corner, making the score 3-0.

The First Half Ends 4-1. After conceding three goals, the British team vowed to counterattack. They advanced from the left, and Parsons made a solo breakthrough. Wu Youliang could not turn around in time, and Yin Zhengda's defense was insufficient. Parsons entered the penalty area and quickly shot the ball, which rolled along the ground and into the net, as the Tung Wah goalkeeper, A-Lu, could not dive for the ball. Soon after, the British goalkeeper, Bowdler, made another mistake, and Chen Hongguang rushed forward and scored. The first half ended 4-1.

Chen Jiaqiu Scores Two More Goals. After the break, the morale of the British team waned. After several back-and-forth plays, Chen Jiaqiu took the lead and scored two more goals, making the score 6-1.

Li Yichen Scores with a Header. At this point, the British goalkeeper was injured and replaced by the right inside defender. The replacement goalkeeper's skills were better than the previous one, and he saved many dangerous shots. Finally, Li Yichen scored with a header, making the final score 7-1. The referee was Li Silian.

Tung Wah Lineup:

Lu Zhongen, Li Ning, Yin Zhengda (replaced by Guan Xun'an), Tu Kaiyuan, Feng Yunyou, Wu Youliang, Wan Xianghua, Chen Hongguang, Li Yichen, Chen Jiaqiu (replaced by Chen Yutian), Cao Qiuting.

British Lineup:

Bowdler, Mathis, Logan, Wickham, Fosgren, Bilett, Parsons, Chubb, Slater, Slejk, Rogers.

Letter to the Editor

To the esteemed Editor of Shen Bao:

We have read a correction published in the Education News Correction column of your newspaper on the 4th of this month, regarding the incident of the 6th District Security Regiment of Jiading County detaining and assaulting students of our school. We find this correction rather laughable. The Regiment's brutality and unreasonableness towards our school's students, the beatings that caused injuries, and the use of handcuffs were witnessed by almost all residents of Huangbo Town that day. Section Chief Xiang of the Education Department, Principal Zheng of Shanghai High School, and Mr. Di Feng from the enemy side came to our school and heard the details firsthand. However, after reading the letter from the Regiment, not only did they deny and conceal their actions with cunning words, but they also falsely accused our students of injuring their sentry soldiers and falsely accused our Principal Teng Songshi of acting arbitrarily and oppressing the Regiment. We students are all young people in our teens, how could we have the courage to injure the Regiment's soldiers who were armed and fierce like tigers and wolves? Our Principal is an educator with no weapon in his hand, how could he act arbitrarily and oppress the Regiment? This is self-evident. The details of the incident, in addition to the report by Principal Zheng of Shanghai High School and Mr. Nishitani to your newspaper's reporter, which reported the truth and was published in your newspaper on the 2nd of this month, have also been thoroughly investigated by officials sent by the county governments and county party headquarters of Jiading and Qingpu counties, who have understood the true situation. The general outline of the incident was also briefly published in the local communications columns of your newspaper, Xinwen Bao, and Shibao on the 6th of this month. At this time, our school can only wait for the official authorities to investigate and handle the matter according to the law. We do not need to refute the Regiment's cunning denials and false accusations. However, we fear that those far away may not understand the true situation, so we specially issue this statement and hope that your newspaper will publish it on our behalf. We wish you good health.

Sincerely,

The Student Self-Government Association of Huangdu Rural Teachers School

New Basketball Techniques (20) (8) (Not Permitted) (to be Reproduced) Original by Claire Burcky, Translated by Zhang Guoxun and Qian Yiqin

The Southern California Trojans had an outstanding record in last season's Pacific Coast Conference. This pivotal offensive method is their winning weapon.

Number 1 first gets the ball and passes it to Number 2. Immediately after, Number 1 goes straight down the sideline behind Number 2. Number 3 immediately goes to the free throw line to act as a pivotal point of reception. After receiving the pass from Number 2, Number 3 turns around and passes it to Number 4, who is diagonally passing behind to the left of Number 3. If Number 4 can remove his (Number 4's) defender, he can directly attack the basket. However, in this situation, the monitoring of the opponent's defenders is extremely strict. Therefore, Number 4 is forced to pass the ball to Number 1, who is advancing along the opposite sideline.

Financial Bar Gold Plunges, Small Rebound

Complex Process, Small Difference. Yesterday, on the last day of the Autumn Race, the gold market was still only open for half a day in the morning. The falling trend of the bar gold slightly subsided, but the trend of a large fall followed by a small rebound was very complex and the difference was not large. Transactions among colleagues in the morning were relatively active but the amount was not large and intentions were hesitant. Afterwards, it rose slightly by one or two taels. The price of silver initially rose slightly due to the US presidential election, but it was not affected by the big news and then fluctuated between 736 and 737 taels. When the foreign exchange rate was stable, it was suddenly reported near noon that Roosevelt was likely to win the US presidential election. As Roosevelt advocated raising the price of silver, a falling trend suddenly started. Sellers were everywhere and it finally dropped to 34 taels and 8 mace. Fortunately, the exchange rate was still stable and rebounded slightly. The Central Bank also sold US dollars to Taikang, Runda, Dadecheng, etc., totaling about 700 bars, which were calculated at US$223. The market will be closed after today's trading. The market situation of the previous session is recorded below.

Although the silver bar rose by one-eighth, the proportional increase was 1 tael and 3 mace (estimated to be between 6 and 7 taels before the market opened). Lyon Raw Silk: Actual Sales Stagnant

｜Silk Fabric Inventories Are Ample... Raw Material Consumption Greatly Reduced｜

French silk fabrics, such as Parisian satin, have a wide sales market and a long-standing reputation in Chinese and foreign markets. Since the global economic instability, French silk exports have long been sluggish. Recently, the political strife in countries such as the United Kingdom and the United States has led to repeated fluctuations in exchange rates, making silk sales even more sluggish. Inventories are piling up, and the consumption of raw silk by various silk weaving factories has been greatly reduced. Actual sales are stagnant, and silk prices have fallen sharply. The current market price for Chinese and Japanese 22-denier silk has fallen by 10 to 20 francs per kilogram compared to mid-September, it is said.

Tunxi Fine Eyebrow Tea: Active European Sales

Yesterday, British merchants such as Xiehe and Jinlong in Tunxi’s high-end fine eyebrow green tea trade reopened due to receiving telegrams from Morocco requesting supply. The entire city negotiated more than a thousand boxes to start trading. The opening market price ranged from 72 to 78 taels. Wuyuan Eastern Route goods were priced at 87 taels, a drop of two to three taels compared to before. There were also slight transactions in Qimen black tea and Gongxi green tea, but selling prices generally trended downward. Currently, although French merchants are showing slight activity, foreign firms are reporting that Japanese and Taiwanese teas are competing aggressively at low prices, and the market is likely to fall rather than rise.

｜Abundant Harvests and Increased Production in Various Regions｜

New tung oil has begun to arrive. In the Jinlan area of Zhejiang Province, several shipments can be produced daily, with a purchase price of 16 yuan per *zhu*. As new goods enter the market, there is not much fluctuation. Chen Oil of Hangzhou firms has already sold out and is urgently preparing for new oil. It is reported that some firms have handled hundreds of shipments of local tung oil from the Jiaxing area at a price of around 20 yuan, to be delivered by cart. The production volume of tung oil in Jiahe and other places will soon peak. This year's harvest has been extremely abundant, so the price of new oil is half as low as last year. However, it is reported that the Shao businesses in that area are heavily involved in tung fruit purchases, initially at 6 yuan 23 cents, later falling to 5 yuan 56 cents, but recently increasing again to 5 yuan 89 cents. Therefore, oil prices are not as weak as they were a few days ago. The cheapest rumored price among local firms is 20 yuan delivered to Shanghai, but according to yesterday's news, it must be 20 yuan and 5 cents. Information from Jingzhou and Yichang in Hubei Province, which are somewhat distant from Shanghai, is not very reliable. However, according to detailed Hankou reports, the harvest is also good, and with the bandits suppressed in various producing areas, the oil mills can also resume their previous operations. It is estimated that this winter's production volume will increase compared to previous years. Furthermore, there is still a lot of old oil in Hankou, and it has recently fallen to 13 taels for Chongjing oil and 12 taels and 34 cents for Pingjing oil. High-quality factory city oil is also at 12 taels and 56 cents, while the lowest quality Tianjin oil is only slightly above 11 taels, but the quality is not very reliable. Local firms have not accumulated much inventory, so they are all focusing on new goods, it is said.

Coal

Zhongxing Coal in Extreme Short Supply

Arrivals of Zhongxing coal have been scarce in the past month, so the amount of coal stored in various warehouses is limited, totaling less than 3,000 tons. Sales have been extremely active recently, with both local and external firms buying in large quantities. Yesterday, the market saw over 500 tons transacted, with prices being exceptionally firm at 11 taels and 25 cents per ton, it is said.

Page 12

Free Talk

"Truly No Bargaining"

— Bi

｜Commercial Transportation｜

"Suzhou people bargain, half price," is a common saying among Shanghai people to describe how shops do not have fixed prices and customers can haggle freely. In fact, the half price of Suzhou people still has a standard, for example, if the asking price is two yuan, haggling down to one yuan is acceptable. However, Shanghai people who mock Suzhou people's half price often bargain for more than double the price. "Ask for the sky, pay on the ground," that is truly absurd.

However, Shanghai people's asking for the sky and Suzhou people's half price are the same in "work" but different in "tune." For the same one-yuan item, Suzhou people ask for two yuan, so the customer bargains down to one yuan, and the deal is done. Shanghai people, on the other hand, use the same method. A one-yuan item, under the golden sign of "Truly No Bargaining," is marked with an original price of ten yuan, and red and green strips of paper are pasted on the large glass window, proclaiming "regardless of cost" and "big sacrifice," "discounted to 90% of the original price." Thus, the customer can also close the deal for just one yuan.

"When entering a country, inquire about its customs." Each place has its own habits, so I have some thoughts and feel that there is an urgent need to promote "commercial ethics," otherwise you will suffer everywhere you go. Therefore, I now hope for "commercial transportation." What is commercial transportation? Well, for example, when we take a train, send a letter, or send a telegram, the price is fixed and unchangeable. Not even a penny less. The gentleman sitting behind the counter, no matter if you call him "sir" or "master," is iron-faced and merciless. You can't expect to get any favors. No matter if you are a local bigwig or a country bumpkin from afar, you are treated the same. So I hope that the bargaining in shops will be like the "truly no bargaining" of transportation agencies.

Also, nowadays, universities and middle schools in Shanghai entrust banks to collect tuition fees, and the bank issues a receipt as a license to attend classes. Thus, rich students and poor students, old and young, are treated equally. As long as the tuition is paid in full, there is no problem. If you can't afford to pay in full, don't even bother to bargain. This spirit of uniformity and no favoritism should be emulated by all merchants, big and small, Chinese and foreign. It would be good to implement commercial education.

Photo Exhibition

— Ding

｜New Works of Several Female Portraits｜

A｜On her neck, it seems that a Shatin pomelo is placed. In the depression of her forward-pointing nose, there are sprinkled some things like fine gauze, which extend to the palms on both sides.

B｜The color of Shandong pears is so much more lovely... But her face is exactly shaped like an inverted Shandong pear. The yellow color on her face feels scary, although there is also the application of stiff powder and soft cream. Also, the small yellow-brown spots on the pears can also be found on her yellow face.

C｜I once saw a German breed of excellent dog at a friend's house. Its long black hair was draped over its white-haired face... Its two black and shiny pupils often shot out a pleasant expression, which I found very endearing. Now, meeting her made me relive the demeanor of that German dog... Because she also has a head of black hair, and it is very long, covering her face made white with cosmetics. But her black pupils do not have that kind of pleasantness.

D｜Equilateral triangles are the outline of her face. The most prominent feature is her pair of shaved and painted long eyebrows... The front ends of the eyebrows almost touch each other, and the outer ends almost curl back. If you look at her from a distance, it looks like she is wearing a thin hairband.

E｜Her companions all call her... "Double-bell alarm clock." Her two eyes, half-open and half-closed, resemble the semicircular double bells covering the top of an alarm clock... Her face is also round... And the sound of her speech is as loud as the simultaneous ringing of double bells.

F｜In her childhood, a large sore that reduced her beauty grew on her left cheek, so it became uneven fleshy warts, very much like a washed, white, round yam. However, her pair of eyes still has captivating authority, if you look at her from the right half.

Standing on the Front of a Tram for a Ride

— Cheng Luding

｜Daydreaming｜

Today, I'm standing on the front of a tram for a ride! I imagine, if I were a great man, if I were a capitalist, if it were summer right now, then I would be happy!

However, after all, it is late autumn, and what is blowing on my face is a cold wind. Even though it is an autumn wind, I am still standing on the front of a tram for a ride.

Standing on the front of a tram for a ride, although not beautiful, and seemingly a ridiculous thing in the eyes of ordinary people, is actually rare and possible. At the very least, it should be a novel ride, right?

I don't know about riding in a car, but whether there is such happiness is still a question. But ultimately, whether there is such a flavor bestowed upon me? Whether there is such scenery accompanying me? Is also a question.

The cold wind blows all over my limbs, the cold wind touches my five senses. Needless to say, the benefits of this ride are definitely more than just this. Even so, it will cause many people to feel elated, and even turn the act of riding into a privilege for the rich.

However, when the piercing autumn wind kisses my face, this is precisely the satisfaction of riding on the front of a tram. It is like being kissed by a modern girl, even if it is, mottled dust, patches of stains, imprinted on my face as a mark of happiness, what difference is there from applying cold cream?

If a shiny car speeds by in front, a cloud of mud and black smoke will fly over from behind. If I am hungry, opening my mouth may also be used as milk and bread. As for scarves and hats, the most practical solution is to ask Mr. Road for help.

In short, it is a joy to ride on the front of a tram. As for mud and sand flying into the eyes to play, as for black smoke flying into the nose to stay temporarily, that goes without saying.

Short Message

— Xiangfei

The Great Wall Records, which has been in preparation for a long time, has now decided to release the first batch of products on New Year's Day of the Gregorian calendar. A total of 46 types are all carefully crafted by famous artists from the North and South. Among them, the "Four or Five Flower Caves" is sung jointly by the four famous female performers and is the most valuable. Yu Shuyan has not recorded for a long time, but the Great Wall actually managed to get him to record, which shows its great influence. The first release includes "Catching and Releasing Cao," and "Stopping at an Inn," excerpts from "The Tassel Meeting." His voice is even more vigorous than before. Other examples include Mei Lanfang and Yang Xiaolou's complete "Farewell My Concubine" (a total of twelve sections recorded, the first two, three, and four sections are released first), Cheng Yanqiu and Wang Shaolou's "Fen River Bay" and "Making a Scene at the Kiln," Shang Xiaoyun and Wang Shaolou's "Wujia Slope," etc., are all perfect matches, wonderful products that are unparalleled for a time. It is heard that record distributors in this and other cities have already eagerly ordered goods from the company.

Crossroads of Death (10)

— Fan Yanqiao

The mailroom sent in a stack of letters. Mu Liang was sorting them. The official documents from various agencies and organizations were quite large and extremely boring. Fortunately, there were small letters in pink, lake blue, and violet, some with fragrance, which diluted the blue indigo smell and the red ink smell. He considered himself specially favored, personally delivering the letters to the female comrades' seats one by one, accepting their standing up to thank him one by one. However, when it came to himself, he did not receive a single heartwarming letter, so he couldn't help but feel envious of the letters sent to the male colleagues. Who would bother to personally deliver them? He pressed the buzzer and called in a messenger, ordering him to distribute them. This was a daily routine that arrived on time every day, which made him feel that the first wife and concubines at home were not only not interested, but also annoying.

Ultimately, is it universal love? Or exclusive love? No, before solving the knotty problems at home, one cannot seek other paths to carry out this loving activity. He made up his mind, and in the waning moon of the second month, he took a week's leave and returned to Suzhou.

The first wife first asked him: "Is work tiring? I heard there are brothels in Fishing Lane, have you been there a few times?"

Mu Liang laughed and said: "Madam! You are too out of touch with the times. Under the National Government, is there still room for brothels to exist?"

The first wife looked unconvinced and said: "Can you really ban them completely? Just look at opium. The more it's banned, the more people smoke it."

Mu Liang said: "There are no official brothels anymore, but if you want to play, there are other ways."

"How so?" The first wife showed that she was good at predicting things.

Aigu also came, not knowing if she was afraid or unable? She didn't say a single meaningful word, just said a simple, straightforward, unanswerable question: "Young Master is back?"

Local News

Nationals Run an Acid Manufacturing Plant

Kaicheng Plant to Start Furnace

Chen Yi to Attend Ceremony

Highly Valued by Various Countries

Kaicheng Sulfuric Acid Plant started its furnace on National Day. The plant is located in the Yinhang District, Jungong Road, covering an area of about 50 acres. It is connected to the Huangpu River in the east, Jungong Road in the west, and is about three miles away from the Zhabei Water and Electricity Plant in the north. The buildings in the plant include offices, material warehouses, storage yards, machine repair shops, and chemical laboratories, as well as special factory buildings such as furnace rooms. In addition to the warehouses, lead rooms, and concentration rooms, there is also an arsenic removal room under construction, and a ore crushing room that only has foundations due to damage to the ore crushing machine. Gao Xingruo and Fang Lixi are responsible for the plant design. Currently, the factory area only occupies one-sixth of the total area, and the remaining area is said to be reserved for the construction of a saltpeter and nitric acid plant and the expansion of the sulfuric acid plant. The raw material, pyrite ore, is purchased from Zhuji and Ruian, and hundreds of tons have arrived and are piled up in front of the furnace room, their brilliant light gleaming like a ground covered in gold. It is said that the products are temporarily set at three types: the "bao acid" produced daily in various lead chambers, with a specific gravity of 50 degrees Baume, which is equivalent to about 62% pure sulfuric acid; the concentrated acid with a Baume degree of 66 degrees, which is about 95% pure acid, is concentrated using a concentrating furnace; and the mixed sulfuric acid with a Baume degree of 60 degrees, which contains about 78% pure sulfuric acid. In addition, various components of dilute acid or concentrated acid can be prepared according to the needs of various manufacturers. Currently, sulfuric acid on the market comes from Japan, and only one type of 66 degrees is available. Factories that use dilute acid must add water to dilute it, which is uneconomical and laborious. After Kaicheng ships its products, there will be various commodities on the market, which is very convenient for user factories. In recent years, many new factories have been established in the country, but the Kaicheng factory, which is operated with domestic capital, uses domestic raw materials, and hires domestic technicians to design, is rare. Therefore, the commercial attachés of various countries in China attach great importance to the company, and several have visited the factory. Sulfuric acid is not only extremely related to industry, but also very important to military affairs. It is said that General Chen Gongxia will soon hold a formal furnace opening ceremony for the plant.

China Merchants Bureau Nationalized

Reorganization Idea from Finance Minister Song

New Candidates Approved by Chiang

Guo Wen She reports: The China Merchants Bureau, the only shipping agency in China, has been decided by the 75th Executive Yuan meeting to be nationalized. All commercial shares will be repurchased by the government, and important figures from the financial world and society will be separately appointed to organize a board of directors and supervisors. Liu Hongsheng has been appointed as the general manager of the bureau. The reorganization principle has been passed by the Central Political Conference yesterday. The information obtained by this agency is compiled as follows:

Origin and Process of Reorganization: The bureau was reorganized by government officials in 1929, and since then, its personnel have changed several times. Recently, the supervisor, Chen Fumu, was criticized for his poor reorganization, and the bureau's financial difficulties have reached an extreme point. Those in charge are unable to turn lead into gold, and the debtors are in dire straits. General Manager Li Guojie recently went to Nanjing and Beijing to make suggestions to Chairman Chiang and the new Minister of Communications, Zhu Jiahua, regarding the reorganization of the China Merchants Bureau. Chiang and Zhu both sympathized with Li's plan, as the bureau has been living on debt for many years. Therefore, Minister Zhu stated a few days ago that the position of general manager would still be held by Li. However, Finance Minister Song Ziwen, noting that the China Merchants Bureau has not made any progress since the National Government sent officials to reorganize it, and that the amount of debt has increased, believes that the reason is insufficient funds. If the China Merchants Bureau is to be truly effective, it must have a large amount of financial resources to reorganize. This reorganization of the China Merchants Bureau is largely Song's idea.

Chiang and Song Discuss Reorganization Candidates: Finance Minister Song Ziwen invited important figures from the banking and financial sectors to his residence in Shanghai this Monday for a final discussion on the reorganization of the China Merchants Bureau (some speculated that Song was borrowing money from the banking and financial sectors, which may have been a misunderstanding). The result was extremely satisfactory. The next morning, he took a plane to Beijing to attend the Executive Yuan meeting and present the reorganization plan, which was approved and forwarded to the Central Political Conference. On the same day, he flew back to Wuhan to present everything to Commander-in-Chief Chiang and submit various plans for nationalization and candidates for the new positions after the reorganization. Chiang expressed that it was feasible to abolish the original position of supervisor and form a board of directors and supervisors, as well as a general manager to preside over the bureau's affairs. Chiang also reviewed this list of candidates and submitted it to the next Central Political Conference for approval and appointment. The investigation conducted by the Guo Wen She reporter yesterday is as follows: Ye Zhuotang, Zhang Shouyong, Shi Liangcai, Zhang Gongquan, Yang Zhixiong, Zhang Xiaolin, Yu Feipeng, Wang Xiaolai, Chen Guangfu, Qian Xinzhi, Hu Bijiang, Li Fuxun, Yu Rizhang, Hu Junzhuang, Sheng Huangyi, Du Yuesheng, Yu Qiaqing, Qin Runqing, Guo Chengen, Huang Jinrong, Rong Zongjing, Jin Tingsun, etc. Liu Hongsheng is the general manager.

Accumulated Surplus May Cause Disputes: Yesterday, the reporter went to the China Merchants Bureau. In addition to the supervisory office preparing to hand over procedures, the general management office was still operating as usual. General Manager Li Guojie also came to the office to work. Then he went downstairs to the Accumulated Surplus Company. According to reports, the company only saw in the newspapers that the government would include all shares and assets of the Accumulated Surplus Company in this principle. The company was not willing to agree. According to another source, the nationalization of the China Merchants Bureau may cause disputes due to the issue of shares of the Accumulated Surplus Company.

Statement of the New General Manager: According to Liu Hongsheng yesterday, he stated that the Executive Yuan meeting had decided to nationalize the bureau and form a board of directors and supervisors, and appointed him as the general manager. He said that in recent years, he has felt very sad about China's shipping industry. The China Merchants Bureau has always had an unclear nature, with issues such as state-owned commercial, commercial-owned commercial, and commercial-owned government-supervised. Now that the government has decided to nationalize it and prepare to repurchase commercial shares, the issue of its nature should be resolved. He said that he has not yet received an order and cannot express his views.

Public Security Bureau Held Winter Defense Meeting Yesterday

Cooperative Defense to Begin on the 16th

Three Defense Zones Each with a Commander

Due to the post-war depression and increasing unemployment in the city, the risk of desperate acts is high during the winter season. Therefore, the municipal public security authorities are taking winter defense more seriously this year than in previous years. Wen Hongen of the Public Security Bureau held a defense meeting at the bureau at 9 a.m. yesterday. Attendees included secretaries, section chiefs, chief inspectors, investigation team leaders, police detachment leaders, district chiefs, precinct chiefs, and heads of fire brigades and security corps from various sections of the Shanghai South area, totaling more than 60 people. Bureau Chief Wen, as chairman, performed the ceremony. First, the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting and the necessity of winter cooperative defense organization. Then, discussions were held and the following resolutions were made: (1) Cooperative defense will begin on the 16th of this month, strictly implementing the winter defense plan of the Garrison Headquarters; (2) The area will be divided into three zones: 1. Shanghai North Zone; 2. Shanghai West Zone; 3. Shanghai South Pudong Zone; (3) Each zone will have a commander: Chen Zhuomin for Shanghai North, Qi Xueqi for Shanghai West, and Wen Hongen for Shanghai South Pudong; (4) When checking household registrations, special attention should be paid to shantytowns and lower-class households; (5) Communication lines on important roads in each zone should be increased to provide security and emergency telephone lines; (6) Suspects should be inspected; (7) Fire brigades should organize equipment and have sufficient protection in case of fire. The meeting adjourned at 11 a.m.

Beixin Bookstore Case

The Municipal Government Has Received Instructions

Will Execute with the Court

The Executive Yuan has instructed the Municipal Government to seal up the Beixin Bookstore with the court in the case of the Beixin Bookstore insulting Islam. The representatives of the Shanghai Muslims who petitioned in Beijing also returned to Shanghai yesterday morning.

Representatives Return to Shanghai: The Shanghai Muslims previously sent Da Pusheng, Mu Huating, Wu Yongxia, Ma Xingdong and other four representatives to petition in Beijing. Except for Ma Xingdong, who had returned to Shanghai earlier to report, the other three representatives took a night train back to Shanghai only after receiving the reply from the Executive Yuan the day before yesterday. They arrived at the North Station at about 8 a.m. yesterday. More than 800 Shanghai Muslims went to the North Station to welcome them. The three representatives got off the train amidst the cheers of the various religious friends and changed to cars and drove straight to the Islamic Association in Qinglian Alley, Fangbang Bridge. Representative Da Pusheng reported on the situation of the petition in Beijing. All the Muslims expressed satisfaction and applauded.

Municipal Government Petition: The Shanghai Muslims elected Ha Shaofu, Da Pusheng, Mu Huating, Wu Yongxia, Sha Peng, Wang Yi and other six people as representatives to carry the reply from the Executive Yuan to the Municipal Government to petition at 10:30 a.m. They requested the Municipal Government to reply to the documents submitted by the heads of the Shanghai Islamic mosques to the Municipal Government as soon as possible and to execute the orders of the Executive Yuan immediately. The Mayor sent Secretary-General Yu to receive them as representatives. First, Ha Shaofu stated the purpose of the petition and presented the reply from the Executive Yuan. Secretary-General Yu expressed his acceptance of the representatives' requests and said that the Municipal Government has received the instructions from the Executive Yuan and will execute them as soon as possible. The representatives expressed their satisfaction and left.

Political Yuan's Reply: The Executive Yuan previously replied to the documents submitted by the heads of the Shanghai Islamic mosques, saying that the book "Little Pig Bajie" published by Beixin Bookstore deliberately spread insults to Islam and should be sealed up immediately, and the publisher, editor and author should be prosecuted according to law, and the Shanghai Municipal Government should be ordered to comply.

Mayor's Talk: The Central News Agency reporter visited Mayor Wu at the Municipal Government yesterday to inquire about the handling of the Beixin Bookstore's insult to Islam case. According to Mayor Wu, the Municipal Government received instructions from the Executive Yuan this morning (that is, yesterday morning) to seal up the Beixin Bookstore with the court. The Municipal Government will naturally comply with the order and will now send a letter to the First Special District Court to order the police to execute the sealing.

Book Industry's Statement: The Shanghai Book Industry Association held an executive committee meeting at 10 a.m. yesterday to discuss the "Little Pig Bajie" case. More than ten executive committee members from Commercial Press, Chung Hwa Book Company, World Book Company, Datong Book Company, Guangyi Book Company, etc. attended the meeting. Li Zhiyun, the manager of Beixin Bookstore, also attended the meeting. It was decided that: (1) A request will be submitted to the central government and the municipal government to handle the "Little Pig Bajie" case fairly in accordance with the law; (2) Beixin Bookstore will be ordered to publish an apology to all Muslims again. The telegrams to the central government and the municipal government were sent yesterday afternoon. Beixin Bookstore has also complied with the order to publish an apology in various newspapers today. The original text reads: "Our bookstore published a collection of folk tales, including a book called "Little Pig Bajie". It mistakenly included Zhu Yangshan's manuscript, "Little Pig Bajie," which was not carefully reviewed. We have repeatedly expressed our apologies to the Muslims. Now, in accordance with the resolution of the Book Industry Association, we formally apologize to all Muslim gentlemen and earnestly hope that you will understand."

Previously Threw Bombs at Residences of Wang Jingwei and Song Ziwen

Tang Youlu Was Indeed Murdered by Him

Hired to Assassinate Lytton

Not Hesitating to Cause an International Dispute

The League of Nations Investigation Team, which came to China to investigate the Manchurian Incident, passed through Shanghai in March. Lord Lytton and other members of the team were also tasked by the League of Nations to investigate the Shanghai Incident nearby, so they stayed at the Cathay Hotel on the Bund to conduct their investigation. Unexpectedly, at this time, some conspirators attempted to cause a major international incident to frame our country. They spared no expense in recruiting traitors and mercenaries to organize an assassination organization, and their followers

were hiding inside the Cathay Hotel, originally planning to throw grenades from the window when key members of the team entered or left the hotel, in order to harm the members. Fortunately, our government and the concession police provided thorough protection, and the plot of these people had no chance to succeed. This kind of conspiracy was not exposed until the 26th of last month, when Chief Inspector You A'gen and Detective Zhou Guisheng of the Lao Zha Police Station arrested 23 people, including Long Lin, in the French Concession, who were heavily implicated in the case of Lu Ziqing, who was kidnapped by bandits on Kunming Road on September 24 and killed on the spot when the kidnapping failed. Wang Jingwei and Song Ziwen were also done by these people. It is now known that Premier Song Ziwen, accompanied by his secretary Tang Youlu, went to the North Railway Station to take a train to the capital last autumn. When they were about to board the train, a bandit suddenly opened fire, killing Mr. Tang with a bullet. The murderer fled the scene immediately. It has now been found that this was also done by Long and his gang. He also gathered his gang on a certain day to go to the municipal government, intending to take the opportunity

to harm Mayor Wu Tiecheng. As for the cases committed by these people in the concession, which were prosecuted by the Public Works Department to the First Special Court, they include: (1) The defendants Long Lin and Tang Ming, from March 20 to 22, carried three grenades and two pistols in the Cathay Hotel on the Bund, plotting to kill Gu Weijun, Song Ziwen, Wu Tiecheng, and Luo Wengan, committing the crime under Article 284, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law. (2) The defendants Long and Tang, at the same time and place, carried guns and ammunition with five accomplices at large, committing the crime of endangering public safety under Article 200, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law, and violating Article 1 of the Gun Control Ordinance promulgated by the National Government in October 1928. (3) The defendant Long Lin, on July 25 last year, gathered a gang at 521 Yuqing Lane, Nanjing Road, to rob Gu Keming of

a total of 16,000 yuan in cash. (4) The defendants Tang Ming and Ma Yijin, on October 2, gathered a gang and broke into 922 Edward Road to rob Zhou Dewen of property worth 258 yuan. (5) The defendants Tang and Ma, on September 22, threatened Cui Xianting at 3 Fuqing Lane, Jing'an Temple Road, with pistols. (6) The defendant Tang Ming sent a threatening letter to He Haiqing on March 19, attempting to defraud him of 400 yuan. Yesterday afternoon, Chief Detective You, who was handling the case, led

Long Lin, Ma Yijin, Tang Ming, Ma Yinhe, Tian Zemin, Weng Xinwu, Chen Chunting, Li Yuncheng, Zhang Chun, Chen Jiesan, He Yinshan, Wan Jiayun, Liu Hanqing, Qin Tianyou, Xiang Ziyun, Xu Hongyuan, Wang Yunqiao, Su Zhian, Wang Bolin, Yu Minghai, Li Zhongfa, Feng Guoqi, and Xiong Zicheng, and others, a total of 23 people, as well as the

one grenade, one pistol, and nine bullets seized, and brought them to the First Criminal Court of the First Special Court, where Judge Qian Hongye took the bench for interrogation. According to lawyer Zhan, there are two reasons for transferring the defendants: (1) The defendants Long Lin and others have been taken to the police station by the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. According to their confession, their sole purpose is to assassinate the highest government officials. Although they all live in the concession, the places where they commit their crimes are in the Chinese territory, such as the attempted assassination of Minister Song at the North Railway Station last year, which resulted in the accidental

killing of Secretary Tang Youlu, and the offense of the defendant Tang Ming waiting near the municipal government to assassinate Mayor Wu. All of these crimes were committed in the Chinese territory, and according to the law, they should be handled by the government agency where the incident occurred without any doubt. (2) If this case is handled by your court, it would not be inappropriate. However, according to the agreement, the investigation procedures of your court should be carried out by the police station, and the only task of the police station is to protect the safety and stability of the concession. It is understandable that they do not have an in-depth study of cases involving political disturbances or having a background, and they are not familiar with such cases. Moreover, the defendants only live in the concession without a fixed address, and

they are not ordinary robbers or murderers. They have absolutely no connection with the security of the concession. Therefore, in order to facilitate the investigation, it should be handed over to the Public Security Bureau for investigation so that the legal facts can be more thoroughly investigated. The police lawyer Gan Jingxian agreed with the Municipal Public Security Bureau's request for transfer and said that this case has political implications and should be handled by the Public Security Bureau. Although the Second Special District Court also sent a letter requesting the transfer, he requested the court to reply to that court and ask them to transfer the case to the Public Security Bureau separately. Judge Qian then approved the request of the lawyer of the Public Security Bureau and ordered that Long Lin and other 23 people be taken away by the personnel of the Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Urgently Hoping for Assistance from Compatriots

On October 7, he arrived at Shangchengzi, that is, Xingyuan Town in Muling County.
